Mr. Moon's Selected Words Volume 3  
Compiled by the Committee for Mr. Moon's Words  

Foreword                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo  

Table of Contents  
  Foreword …………………………………………………… 3  
1) When Will I Stand Before the Father?  
John 3:1-21  
<Prayer>  
Father of Mercy! Please appear with the light of life over this valley of death. Father of Love! Please appear with love in this wilderness like a wasteland. Father of Glory! Please appear as a glorious gift over the dry souls who are thirsty. Almighty Father, I earnestly wish and hope that this time may be allowed for the dead lives to kneel before Your altar. Please allow us to awaken this sleeping nation, and let the sons and daughters who are asleep in confusion rise up quickly to awaken humanity. Thus, may the gathering sons and daughters raise the torch of life to lead the nation before You, and may the day of joy when all of humanity is led before You come quickly, Father. Today, as I come before Your knees, please allow me to reflect on myself and to examine whether I am prostrating before Your holy presence with a sanctified body. If there are any faults that are not worthy before Your will, Father, please shine the light of life into our hearts so that we may repent. Please hold our bodies with the power of the Holy Spirit so that we may be liberated from sin and experience the resurrection.  
Each of us must be able to take responsibility before You while also being able to inherit Your eternal legacy at this time, which is September 8, 1957, at the former headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).  
When Will I Stand Before the Father?  
I earnestly wish and hope that this time may be allowed for us to inherit Your eternal legacy. Thus, please allow us to experience all the circumstances that are deeply connected to Your heart at this time, and I earnestly hope and wish that each person gathered here may be entrusted with an inner mission. Please forgive all that we have done wrong during the week, and if we have come before You with hearts and bodies that You do not desire, Father, please scrutinize us with Your fiery eyes. Please allow this time to be one where we can confess everything before the dignified Father and be able to repent before You. On this day, please work uniformly upon the sons and daughters who are scattered in the regions, fighting alone while holding the torch of Your words. May the loving hand of the Father be abundantly manifested upon their heads and in their hearts, guiding them so that they lack nothing in pioneering through the dark environment. Please do not allow all the words of life that have been proclaimed under Your guidance to fall to the ground, and now, may the sons and daughters who have been in darkness receive the gift of resurrection through Your words. Please establish these sons and daughters as the lords of life for this nation, and I earnestly hope and wish that they may live exemplary lives in the gifts of joy. I earnestly ask that You work uniformly upon all the altars where the sons and daughters are building lonely altars and gathering in Your name. Thus, may the day of joy when we unite within the realm of heavenly ideals, moving towards one world, one purpose, and one goal come quickly. I earnestly ask that You govern from the beginning to the end of this time, and I pray in Your name. Amen.  
<Words>  
The title of the message I wish to think about with you is "When Will I Stand Before the Father?" I will speak briefly on this title.  
The attitude of a true believer who must stand before the Father  
Human beings living on this earth, no matter how excellent or capable they may be, are beings born with the bloodline of corruption. In other words, they carry original sin. Therefore, humans have gone through the history of sin until now, and they have traversed the path of struggle against evil in this world or the universe, a struggle that may be known or unknown. And when we hope for a day of hope, there are countless conditions of the wilderness that block that path, which you must have experienced in your life or life journey.  
So, what must we do to be liberated in such an environment? You must know that this has been the aspiration and standard sought by conscientious and good people throughout history. However, if "my today" is to be better than "my tomorrow," we must absolutely draw the existing God into our realm of life. In other words, we must recognize God not merely as a logical or conceptual God but as a tangible God in our lives. This is a critical issue for us believers.  
Because humans are fallen, there remains a path that they must take to escape the fate of corruption. Many prophets and sages have exerted their sincerity, patience, and intelligence on this path that humans must take, but that path has not yet been fully traversed and remains as a cosmic path of destiny. Moreover, the barriers created by the sins committed by humans are not few, and they are endlessly blocking the way, and we are in a position where we must break through them.  
Humans standing in this position have yearned for the object of faith, that is, the absolute God, the absolute existing being, but they have felt that they do not know various aspects of this. Therefore, you must not recognize God's existence vaguely and conceptually. However, if you recognize God's existence only from a logical standpoint, it would be unreasonable. This is because God is not confined to the realm of logic. When we ask whether a faith that recognizes God logically can lead our lives to complete the reality of eternal life, there are many problems.  
So, how can we, living in such an environment today, go before the true Lord and the Father? We must understand that our desire to approach the Father is both the historical hope of humanity and the goal of God's providence.  
Then, when we find ourselves in such an environment and seek God and the path of faith, what will block our way? First, doubts that arise unknowingly will block the path. Also, the trials of sin will block the way, and the power of death that unexpectedly assaults us will block our path. We must overcome the peaks of doubt, the peaks of sin, and the peaks of death.  
And each person has harbored the desire for an eternal ideal to be connected and for that connection to govern their life and purpose. Furthermore, humans have unconsciously longed for a standard through which they can establish such an eternal relationship. Humans must go through this process.  
You also wish to experience God's existence within your realm of life and yearn to meet God's reality. However, when you try to set God's reality as the object of faith, there will be many doubts. However, you must not be unable to move forward due to those conditions of doubt, and you must pass through them. You must also feel that you are under the great shadow of death.  
So, what should you do after feeling this? If you just hold these issues in your heart, you cannot walk the true path of faith. There is no way to solve these problems. If you acknowledge that God exists, you must be able to remain as an object of faith who honestly presents all your doubts to God. You must also be able to honestly confess all your sufferings from sins, including both the transgressions you have committed and the inherited genetic sins.  
Moreover, even though you are in a position where you must fight against everything that blocks your way, and even though you must take steps toward the world of eternal hope, and even though you must enter the promised heaven where you can feel the ideal of eternal life, you must overcome the fact that you are still in the powerless realm of death.  
The way to resolve doubts—courageous faith  
Now, if you have a desire to seek God the Father, you must cast out the doubts, sins, and death you have carried until now. The place where you have remained, in connection with the history of sin, is not an environment where you can relate to God or goodness. The environment in which you can become good must be a new environment, not that one.  
So, how can you escape this environment? You must have a heartfelt desire that says, "I am in this insufficient state, so please accept me, Father." When such a heart takes root in you, you will be able to enter the world of eternal life.  
And you must be able to put forth the doubts you have from your surrounding environment and say, "Father, please remove this from our bodies and hearts," and you must have the courage to leave your sinful self before the Father or any subject of faith just as you are. If not, you must at least establish such a heart at the center of your mind and think about it. If you cannot do that, you cannot walk the path of faith.  
When God comes to humans, what condition does He present? He presents faith. Therefore, humans must break away from all that causes doubt and create an environment where they can believe, organize the environment of sin, and create an environment of goodness, and break through the environment of death to establish an environment of life.  
Only after doing all these things can we sing of God's infinite glory centered on God's eternal love and reveal God's authority. This is the time that humanity has longed for. No one can deny this fact. Today, we must ruthlessly clear away the sinful environment in which we find ourselves. We must also be able to lay everything before the Father, clarify all the doubts that have existed in our relationship with the Father, break down all the elements of sin we have carried, and have the standard of faith to be liberated from the power of death.  
So, what must we do? We must find the way to resolve our doubts. We must find the way to life. If such a way does not exist in the human world, then God cannot come. If God is the existing being who stimulates our conscience to realize our mistakes and repent, then you must establish the highest hopes, life, and standards of humanity that God desires.  
The day when this will be possible, the historical end times will inevitably come. So, in light of this cosmic path of destiny, how much have you contemplated? In fact, today you are in an environment where you can harbor doubts about the universe, this society, the world, and even yourself.  
The central being who can resolve all these problems is God. And the only one who knows everything that humans are curious about is God, and the only one who can solve it is the one absolute being, God.  
Therefore, you must bear all these cosmic doubts related to you and say, "O God, I now come with all my doubts about the universe; if there is a heavenly relationship between You and me, I believe that You will not forsake me, so please resolve all these doubts." You must have the courage to entrust it to God.  
When you find yourself in a position where you cannot resolve such doubtful issues, if you recognize resolving them as a duty of faith and struggle to resolve them, you may walk alone but ultimately reach a position beyond ordinary believers.  
When we try to open the path of evil while blocking the path of goodness, we must confess all our doubts before the subject of faith. The act of confession itself can be considered sacred, and when you sincerely call out to Heaven, "Father! God!" with the sincerity to challenge the limits of your cosmic consciousness, the Father must respond to you. God has a responsibility to respond to such a person.  
Truth does not violate heavenly principles, and what is true will not be forsaken by God. Therefore, you must have the determination to hold onto God with a sincere heart, a heart of loyalty, and a heart of devotion to resolve all the doubts in your heart.  
If this doubt is not resolved, we have no way to break through the path of sin. No matter how great the grace we receive, if the doubt is not completely resolved, we can stumble again.  
Reflecting on the origin of the fall, Adam and Eve fell because they doubted. Therefore, for us who are in the process of restoration, we must resolve any doubts we have. The greater the doubt, the more our hearts are bound. Thus, we must become people who have the courage and determination to boldly approach God to resolve our doubts.  
Throughout history, humans have strived to resolve many questions regarding their views on life and the universe. However, those questions have not yet been completely resolved.
14   When will I stand before my father? This question has not been clarified. Now, to clarify that which is in question, a person who challenges this issue head-on and comes forth with a faithful appearance before heaven, pouring out all their sincerity, will be established by God, and their questions will also be resolved. Throughout a long history, numerous prophets have come and gone to reveal the secrets of heaven’s providence. However, the overall content that humanity has been curious about has not been clarified. Therefore, Jesus had to come to clarify these cosmic questions, to resolve the unresolved sins of humanity, and to address the issue of death. The only one who could resolve these questions of humanity, death, and sin was Jesus. And Jesus lived a life of truth for God more than anyone who came during the 4,000 years of historical process. He transcended himself to clarify cosmic doubts, labored for the glory of the universe beyond his own glory, and sacrificed infinitely to fulfill God’s will without caring for anything of his own. Because of such a consistent heart and life, Jesus Christ was established as the foremost pioneer before heaven, representing history. Thus, after breaking through the barriers of historical doubt, Jesus confidently proclaimed, “Believe in me.” How could this one statement of Jesus, “Believe in me,” become a standard of faith, and why did Jesus establish this standard of faith? Knowing that it takes time to clarify so many questions, Jesus spoke in such a way to introduce a path that would naturally be understood at some point. Jesus knew not only about the affairs of humanity on earth but also about the heavenly world. Therefore, Jesus said, “If I have told you earthly things and you do not believe, how will you believe if I tell you heavenly things?” (John 3:12). Human words cannot cross the peak of doubt. All questions can only be clarified through the words of heaven. So when can we hear the words of heaven? That time is the final time when humanity comes forth, the final judgment day spoken of in Christianity. God has been carrying out all restoration providence based on that time. However, when a new word that removes all conditions and elements of doubt, death, and sin appears on this earth, the question becomes whether you yourselves are able to receive that word. If you wish to accept such a word, you must become a person who is as devoted to Jesus as Jesus was devoted to heaven. Just as a vessel is needed to receive a precious gift, when the word that clarifies the overall questions appears in the future, you must be in a position to receive it. 

The way to connect with God
So how can we receive this word? It is through your sincerity and devotion. Just as Jesus was faithful to heaven on behalf of the 4,000 years of history, you must be faithful to heaven and Jesus on behalf of the 6,000 years of history. If you do not become such a person, you cannot possibly step into the era of overall clarification. Then what kind of word will this clarifying word be? It will manifest as a new word that you have not heard before. And what kind of word will this be? This word will be one that can clarify not only personal questions but also questions about the world and the universe. What kind of system will this word have? It is difficult to express in one word, but to put it roughly, it will be a word with concrete content that can clarify the history of questions that have flowed for 6,000 years. In the future, such a word with concrete content will appear. And when we apply that word to our personal lives, it will manifest as a word that can govern our living environment, and through that word, the authority of the absolute being governing the eternal world will be closely related to our lives. That word must have such concrete content. Therefore, when we become one with that word that is unified with God, no doubt, death, or sin can invade that unified place. And that word must be an absolute word that can complete our faith. It must also be a word that can lead us to pursue absolute goodness and make us feel eternal life. 

Looking at the history of truth-seeking that humanity has pursued until now, the initial object of human inquiry was the universe. In other words, humans have been pondering the question, “What is this universe?” After that, they have focused on humanity itself, pondering the question, “What is a person?” In this way, humans have been seeking truth centered on reason, but is that reason perfect? No, it is not. Reason alone cannot be perfect. And that reason cannot enhance absolute values, nor can it become the eternal ideal of human life. Thus, humans have come to acknowledge the absolute being, that is, God, religiously. However, that God was a humanistic God to ask for forgiveness for the sins humans have committed. He could not be a God who transcends logic and relates to individual humans. He was, after all, a God based on human thought. However, this view of God is not a complete view of God. 

Taking a step further from this perspective, true believers acknowledge the absolute God. However, while they acknowledge the absolute God, they do not realize that they have not established a relationship with that God in their faith life. They remain in a logical position and cannot resolve the question of how to experience the existence of God in a way that relates to their lives. We must have an ideology that can resolve this. And that ideology must replace cosmology, replace the value of human reason, replace the value of human life, and connect to the ideology of the absolute being, that is, the ideology of God. Such an ideology must relate to us. It cannot be achieved by any human expression. It cannot be achieved through any human personality cultivation. 

The standard of faith to meet God
Now that we have been born into the new ideological realm of heaven, we must seek the cosmic ideology during our lifetime. We must recognize that Jesus is the one who passed through the ideology of God, and we must reach a level where we can automatically believe and know that Jesus, who stands on the highest standard of conscience and the highest standard of goodness, represents the entire character of God. Why are we not becoming like Jesus? It is because the environment we are currently in is strongly pushing against our hearts that want to do something. People forget this fact. Even if my conscience is directed toward the highest goodness, that heart does not smoothly translate into action. Why is that? Because, as a consequence of the fall, this world has become a world of sin. A force of darkness stronger than the power of our true heart and nature is suppressing us. This force of darkness is what Christianity calls Satan. We cannot help but think about how to overcome this force of darkness. 

The forces of darkness and the elements of evil within our bodies lead us to harbor doubts and engage in sinful actions, dragging us into the world of death. We must have an environment that can block and push this away. The religion that seeks to establish such an environment is Christianity. Therefore, just as Jesus stepped forward to believe in God, He told us, “Believe in me.” That “me” refers to the “I” who accomplished this, but who will carry out the movement to create such individuals and expand them into the human world? This cannot be done by human power. It must be done by God. However, human faith is needed here. In other words, just as Jesus overcame the forces of darkness surrounding him by believing in God, when we believe in God, Satan may momentarily appear in our work and where we move, but ultimately, heaven will appear and drive Satan away. To establish this one standard, Jesus set the conditions of faith. 

So, to establish the conditions of faith, to what standard must we believe? You should not believe only to the extent that you can imagine. You must not believe only to the extent of your thoughts. That standard is not the standard of faith believed in today’s world. If you are to believe in the existence of the great and high God, you must establish a standard of faith that can be compared to the value of that great and high God. 

So to what extent can we say that humans currently believe? The level of that belief is very low, as Jesus said, “If I have told you earthly things and you do not believe, how will you believe if I tell you heavenly things?” (John 3:12). Jesus made a disheartening statement about the level of human belief. Then, can people of faith today establish a standard of absolute faith? This is the question. Until now, Christianity has only believed in God within the Bible. However, even within God, there is faith. Since God Himself has an infinite ideology of creation, there is a belief to realize that ideology. God Himself believes in something. Therefore, we must pursue infinite faith. If we possess such faith, we can believe all the words contained in the Bible. 

Furthermore, to believe all the words in the Bible, you must be able to think of the words that Jesus could not say while he was on earth. Thus, by finding the parts that Jesus did not speak, you can cross over the peak of cosmic doubt and comfort the ancestors who have passed through cosmic death, suffering, and sin. Although you currently believe in the Lord who is the subject of faith, you must not stop at just believing in Jesus. You must establish a relationship and connection with Jesus through the conditions of that faith, placing eternal life on the line. And you must feel the existence of God on the foundation of the relationship of faith you have established with Jesus. If you truly believe in Jesus, you will be able to accomplish such things. 

Those who explore the path of infinite faith can achieve infinite development. Today, ordinary Christians do not know this fact. You must understand that heaven is waiting for true believers who are captivated by the ideology of infinite faith and wish for the realization of heaven. 

True believers are not influenced by evil environments
Now you must be able to pass through the conditions of life on your path of faith and be able to pass through the secrets of heaven’s providence, so you must seek to establish such a path. After passing through those, you must cross over the peaks of doubt, the peaks of sin, the peaks of death, and all the peaks of desires centered on evil. 

Then, after crossing all those peaks, what should you do? Next, we must welcome God. We must be able to invite the one who is the subject of faith, the subject of goodness, and the subject of life into our hearts. This is the state of unity that Jesus spoke of when He said, “In that day you will know that I am in my Father, and you in me, and I in you” (John 14:20). How wonderful it is to believe in the Creator God who has infinite hope and to place that God in your heart and be at ease? You must understand that God desires us to become such beings. 

The facts of the spirit world cannot be recorded in just a few books; there is so much content that it cannot be contained even in tens of thousands of books. The spiritual world that has been shown and taught to humans until now is only a part, so the books that introduce the spiritual world until now cannot clarify the entire spiritual world. Is the word recorded in the Bible the entirety of the faith journey that humans must take, or does it contain the content that can restore the entirety of value? I would say no. Some may curse me for saying this, but… Therefore, we were told to believe in Jesus as a condition of faith, and God has worked in various ways to make humans believe that Jesus is the one with the greatest value. 

Thus, the more we believe in Jesus and establish a relationship with Him, the more directly God can govern our lives, and by receiving God’s governance, we can connect with God’s value from the position of being God’s object and establish a heartfelt relationship with God. In this way, God’s truth can also manifest in our lives, and we possess elements that are in contrast to God’s truth. Ultimately, we must build a living environment that can integrate all ideologies and unify all nations. Only by entering such a living environment can we have hope for goodness, possess the life of goodness, and manifest the absolute value of goodness. When humanity stands in such a position, God can appear not as the God of a particular nation but as the God of all creation. If you do not become that way while you are alive, you cannot become the direct sons and daughters of God. 

Today, you have already embarked on the path of not being like others. You are already walking the path of not being like others. And you are believing with the standard of faith placed on the personality of the cosmic Creator. When you achieve the standard of your faith, the elements of evil will disappear from you. When that happens, you will be able to digest everything in this world. 

Even if the truth is alongside evil, it does not change under the influence of that evil.
21. Therefore, no matter how bad the environment is, if you become a true son or daughter of God, you will not be dominated by that environment. If you do not become such a true believer, you will not only be unable to face the heavenly principles, but you will also be unable to stand before God. Then why did Jesus call Himself the only begotten Son of God? The reason Jesus presented conditions that are incredibly difficult for humans to believe is to grant them the benefit of being able to leap forward momentarily if they believe this. Thus, when humans believe in Jesus with infinite faith and sincerely cry out to heaven, their faith will grow exponentially. The higher the degree of your faith toward the center of heaven, the greater the spiritual world can work through you, and if you possess infinite faith, you can simultaneously feel facts of the super-sensory world and the universe that you cannot even imagine through your character. However, humans have lost these amazing things. If the attitude of a believer is to aim for an infinite world that must be traversed, then in the end, we must engage in a cosmic battle to drive away those who are crying out for a faith that remains within a limited realm. To become true sons and daughters who can stand before God, looking at the historical path so far, we see that the numerous prophets and sages who came to introduce a new era were almost all driven away. Those who drove them away were our ancestors. When Jesus came, the Jews disliked and opposed Him. They did not know. They believed that what they believed was the best and judged the providence of salvation, which represented the universe and heaven, in their own way. In this way, our ancestors have repeatedly committed the error of opposing the path of heavenly principles and breaking the history of heavenly principles. 

So, who can possess a hundred percent faith at this end time? You who have embarked on the battle to repel sin must stand in such a position. And on the basis of that faith, you must practice with a thorough sense of responsibility. 

22. When will I stand before the Father? You must practice with endless effort. If you do not stand in this position, you cannot stand as a qualified object before the one who comes in the name of the bridegroom with the ideal of infinite love, nor can you establish a relationship with God, who commanded to multiply and be fruitful infinitely. From this perspective, what is sin? It is not believing. Not believing in the person sent by God is sin, and not believing in His words is also sin. Therefore, you must accept the cosmic ideals of God. And you must go forth with firm faith. However, when you try to go forth with such faith, doubts that are contrary to it will arise in your heart. This is because the forces of evil are at work in your heart. Those forces of evil make you feel fear and terror. Therefore, you must not have a faith that is swallowed by those evil forces. You must go forth with the capacity to digest and overcome such things. Jesus stood in such a position, which is why He did not shy away from the place of bearing the cross. Who can criticize such Jesus? A person who truly believes in God cannot possibly criticize Jesus. 

In the same position as Jesus, we must seek a new path of faith. If we sincerely walk a new path of faith, we will find empirical facts, facts related to God, and facts connected to God. In doing so, we will be able to find the way to realize the ideals of the Creator, who desires unity. Today, you who have set out on a new path of faith, prepared to face death, if you go forth with absolute faith toward God's hope, you can find Godly values through that path of faith. Therefore, you must feel a sense of responsibility with such faith and become true practitioners who practice with such faith. Without becoming such individuals, you cannot stand before the Father. You cannot stand as true sons and daughters before the absolute Father, nor can you stand as loyal subjects. 

Now, in order to stand as true sons and daughters before the absolute Father, we must overcome all the worlds of doubt, all the worlds of death, all the worlds of sin, and all the worlds of fear. If we understand the content of faith that heaven demands, we must establish a standard that can prove it and stand before heaven. Otherwise, it will be impossible to become true sons and daughters of God. When you step forward with such faith, you can establish an eternal relationship with God, enjoy eternal goodness and eternal life, and receive eternal liberation from suffering, allowing you to live within the eternal kingdom of heaven. 

<Prayer> At one time, we entrusted this world to faith that relies solely on God, but it all collapsed. After that, we tried to find this land through human reason, but now it has become evident that the will cannot be fulfilled through that either. Therefore, we must rely on heaven and also on humans, and we cannot help but feel that there are parts that must be accomplished through the cooperation of heaven and humanity. 

Father, do not leave us to ourselves. We know that humanity has walked a historical path filled with failures. We know that faith alone is not enough, nor is it enough to rely solely on ourselves. We hope to have a cosmic ideal and truth that can transcend ourselves and find the origin of our lives. We also recognize that we must establish a standard through which heaven can come to us while we have a place, so please guide us to the position where we can call You Father from a standpoint of complete understanding through the absolute path of faith. 

Jesus told us to seek Him in the relationship of bridegroom and bride. The heart that can communicate internally is the heart, and the word that allows us to communicate internally is the word. Therefore, please allow us to communicate through the word, and through that word, let us know the truth and the heart, and through the ideological ideals, let us be able to know God's heart. 

24. When will I stand before the Father? I earnestly wish to be allowed to be connected to the position where I can know God's heart through ideological ideals. I sincerely hope and desire this. Father, please do not allow us to remain in extremely narrow circumstances today, and do not let us become foolish by losing our overall value due to being swayed by trivial matters. 

While admiring the greater grace of the Father, allow us to behold the greater heavenly personality of the Father, and since that personality has not yet appeared on this earth in any form, and heaven desires that such a personality be manifested through us, please allow us to move before the Father with a greater standard of faith and with a sincere heart and devotion that is in accordance with that ideal, and guide us to fulfill that responsibility, Father, I earnestly hope and desire this. 

Father, at this time, please grant the final grace that You wish to bestow, and as sons and daughters of the glorious Father, through a sacrificial life, let us accept the eternal ideals of faith of the eternal Father as the ideals of our daily lives, and guide us to become victorious figures who can boast before all people. I earnestly hope and desire this, Father. 

Please implant all these words as the source of life in their hearts, and help those words to work within their hearts. I earnestly ask this in the name of the Lord. Amen. 

2) Let us become true sons and daughters of the True Father 
Romans 8:12-30 

<Prayer> Father! We have gathered again today before Your knees after fighting in the place of evil for a week with the gifts You have granted. Please accept us even if we are lacking. We have come out as objects of Your concern, so compassionate Father, powerful Father, and loving Father, do not leave us as we are. We cannot do without Your care. Countless satans are surrounding us and seeking our lives, so Father, please protect us. Today, may our individual selves be submerged in Your deep love and be allowed to sing of Your glory in our hearts, and may this hour be one in which we can bow down and worship before You, Father, I earnestly hope and desire this. 

During the week, we know that actions that have not been permitted remain in our lives, and there are many elements that cannot appear before Your will, so compassionate Father, powerful Father, please manifest with the authority of victory, and I earnestly hope and desire that You grant us the hand of re-creation once more. 

Father! This day is a holy day, so please bless the numerous denominations gathering on behalf of the thirty million nations, and may the lonely sons and daughters who are building hidden altars to fulfill Your one will also bow down before You at this time. 

26. Let us become true sons and daughters of the True Father. We know that there are many who are gathered here today, so please work uniformly upon them and grant them the final grace that You have promised at the end. 

Thus, they may be able to build the final altar of victory and establish Your glory over the Korean Peninsula, Father, I earnestly hope and desire this. Now, your sons and daughters gathered in this place entrust everything to You, so please accept us as living sacrifices and guide even one life not to stray from Your will. Even if we are attacked by satan, please allow us to be true sons and daughters who can boldly call You my Father. I earnestly hope and desire this. 

Today, there are lonely sons and daughters fighting difficult battles scattered in various regions, so please raise the power of Your re-creation in every place they gather, allowing them to testify that they are Your sons and daughters. Beloved Father, I earnestly hope and desire this. Now, I earnestly ask that You take charge of all the content we offer during this hour. 

<Word> The title of the message I want to give you is "Let us become true sons and daughters of the True Father." I will speak for a moment with this title. 

God's hope for humanity is that the God who created all things has not abandoned this fallen world and has been solely responsible for it while engaging in a fierce battle against satan until now, as you all know well. What could be the highest purpose that God desires? What does He want? Even after going through countless historical processes of sorrow, what is the content that He has not abandoned humanity but has embraced? It is that God wants to say to humanity, "You are My true sons and daughters." 

To achieve this ideal, God has fought until now. In the garden of God's goodness, where all things harmonize centered on God's love in glory, Adam, who was qualified to call God, "My Father! Receive glory," lost that value due to the fall. Therefore, you must understand that God desires to hear the voice of His original sons and daughters calling Him "Father" since the beginning of creation. The Father we call today is not the kind of Father who is called from the standpoint of sin. Therefore, we must escape from the world of sin and enter the garden of goodness. 

That ideal garden is a world where humans can manifest God's glory while living in joy. <Word> Today, I will briefly speak to you under the title, "Let us become brides who restore what Jesus cast aside." 

The Jesus who was forsaken on this earth. The Jesus whom humanity has believed in until now, or the Jesus whom many people in this era welcome and call Christ and Lord, did not receive such glory when He came to this earth. You must understand well that none of the people at that time believed in the words Jesus left behind as heavenly words, nor did anyone believe them as words that replaced their lives. 

Although Jesus came for the earth, He was not welcomed by the people on the earth. No one truly welcomed Him on behalf of individuals, and no one welcomed Him on behalf of families. You must understand this. Jesus lived thirty years in the household of Joseph and Mary, but no one in that family understood the heart Jesus held, the hope Jesus desired, or what Jesus's life and work should be. Furthermore, no one understood the deep meaning of the words Jesus spoke and welcomed Him as the Christ. Instead, the family of Jesus took a position of disbelief and rejection. 

There was a providential mission that should have been established in the family, a mission that should have been established for individuals, and a mission that should have been established through life and work, but among the Jewish people at that time, there was no one who felt Jesus's mission as their own. Even though everything Jesus saw, heard, spoke, and did was in ignorance on the earth, His life was not solely for the people on the earth; He lived for the new will of God that humanity did not know. Therefore, you must understand that Jesus, who lived for this new heavenly will, had a hidden sorrow behind His words, ideas, actions, and life. 

Moreover, as Jesus could not establish His will in the family, He desired for His will to be known through society or through denominations. However, Jesus was not welcomed by Judaism or the people of Israel and was rejected. Thus, not only was Jesus's person rejected, but also the words He spoke were rejected, and everything He did and wanted to do was rejected. You must understand this. 

Therefore, you must be able to comprehend the heart of Jesus, who was forsaken, the loneliness He felt when rejected, and how great the pain inscribed in His heart must have been. If you become someone who does not know such suffering of Jesus, you cannot possibly manifest as someone who knows the life, ideology, actions, and words of Jesus, who bore the responsibility of 4,000 years of history. 

Today, we know a little of Jesus's situation through the biblical words that reflect this, but that knowledge is merely intellectual. It is only what we have heard and understood with our ears. However, this is not enough. When Jesus preached to the Jewish people of Israel long ago, they only listened with their ears and understood with their heads. Because they could not experience it in their real lives, they made Jesus walk the path of the cross. Therefore, you must clearly understand that merely knowing the words with your head and ears is not sufficient. 

So, what should we do today? We must not only know the words we have heard with our heads...
86   We must become brides who seek to restore what Jesus had lost, and at the same time, we must know and act with our hearts. However, during that time, until Jesus walked the path of death on the cross, there was not a single person who understood His words with both head and heart and acted accordingly. Among the people of Israel, the Jewish faith, and even among the disciples whom Jesus had taught with all His heart for three years, no one appeared who understood this; they all found themselves in a position of disbelief. Jesus taught with all His sincerity, revealed God's intentions through dreams, and earnestly enlightened those who were ignorant of God's providence by saying, "Anyone who has seen me has seen the Father," yet the beloved disciples of that time were completely unaware of the circumstances behind Jesus. There was not a single person who understood His words with their head, felt them with their heart, and acted upon them with their body.

The Qualification and Mission of Jesus' Bride

So what is our responsibility in this historical end time? We must recover all the ideals of Jesus that have been lost, fight against all the sins on this earth and achieve victory to build the world of heaven, and we must qualify ourselves to welcome Jesus as our bridegroom. It is not enough to merely hear and know about Jesus; we must understand with our heads, feel with our hearts, and experience with our bodies.

Therefore, you must understand that among the words spoken by Jesus, there was a deep sorrow in His heart because He could not fully reveal the Father's will to the people of that time, nor could He disclose the secrets of heavenly principles. If you do not understand such circumstances and feelings of Jesus, you will not be able to truly comprehend His words, nor will you understand the life He lived to establish those words, nor the work He undertook to save all humanity.

At that time, there was an infinite difference between the heart of Jesus and the hearts of the people He faced. Jesus could not express the words deeply embedded in His heart and only spoke words of counsel to awaken the ignorant people. So what were the contents of the words Jesus spoke at that time? They were words of counsel to those who lived in a world of Satan, an evil land, and among enemies, but who aspired to become children of heaven. They were words that presented a way to overcome trials without being tested in the world of Satan. In other words, Jesus left behind a stepping stone for all people to keep His words in the world of Satan and to live in place of His heart.

Thus, what final words did Jesus leave for us? He said, "You are my bride." At that time, Jesus could not speak directly to His beloved disciples but had to speak from a position of promising the future. You must understand this heart of Jesus. His love for His disciples, the nation of Israel, and Judaism remained unchanged in light of the heavenly will entrusted to Him. However, because the people were ignorant, the denominations were ignorant, and the disciples were ignorant, Jesus bore all the arrows alone as a vanguard fighting against Satan and walked the path of suffering to pave the way for them. In other words, you must clearly understand that Jesus was a sorrowful figure who could not find an environment in which to express the deeply hidden feelings of His heart and the ideals of the heavenly bridegroom and bride.

Then, as Jesus left us with the hope of a joyful day on this earth by saying, "You are my bride," what has become of that bride's ideal today? Even after thousands of years of history and fierce battles against Satan, not a single person has entered the position of Jesus' bride. Therefore, today, you must become the bride who seeks to restore what Jesus had lost.

You must establish the ideals of the bride that Jesus desired, which the chosen Israel could not establish, and which His beloved disciples could not establish, and you must become someone who can face the heart of Jesus.

So from what position did Jesus speak His words? They were words spoken from a position that had not yet completed the ideals of the bride. His words were left behind so that believers could truly qualify as the bride and connect with Jesus' earnest circumstances. Therefore, we must fulfill the true meaning of the words given by Jesus today, become the bride that Jesus desires, and advance to the position where we can experience the inner feelings that Jesus felt at that time. If no one reaches such a position, you must understand that the purpose of the words Jesus spoke throughout His thirty years of life will not be fulfilled.

The Circumstances of Jesus During His Public Ministry

So what was the situation when Jesus preached on this earth? The people did not welcome His words but opposed Him and even persecuted Him. Therefore, today, you must become someone who can empathize with the inner feelings of Jesus, who spoke for those who persecuted Him even in such a situation, and you must be able to feel the heart of Jesus, who is the bridegroom of all people. 

Moreover, you must have the feeling that the inner heart of Jesus, which He expressed 2000 years ago, resonates in your heart, body, and mind today, and you must become someone who can comfort Him. Thus, you must welcome the words that were rejected at that time and become a saint who will surely fulfill the purpose of Jesus' words on this earth.

The words of the bridegroom Jesus have been passed down to us through many historical hardships, but how should you respond to those words today, in this end time? You must not only know those words with your head but also understand them with your heart and body. 

You must also understand that while Jesus' words were rejected, His thirty years of life as a sacrifice were also rejected. In other words, it is not only that Jesus' words were rejected, but that Jesus Himself was rejected, and because He was rejected, His thirty years of life were also cast aside. 

So what should you do today, as someone who must become Jesus' bride? You must be able to reclaim the thirty years of life that Jesus was rejected from within your own being. Jesus lived for thirty years in the home of Joseph, but no one welcomed what He was doing, and He could not live in an environment where He could go wherever He wanted. There was a stark difference between His intentions and words and the life He lived. Because He could not find a single being to whom He could express His circumstances, Jesus lived silently as a carpenter, unable to say all that He wanted to say.

Furthermore, Jesus was the protagonist who could fulfill the will that God had intended by sending many prophets. At that time, Jesus was the center of the nation, the center of the denomination, and not only the center of individuals but the representative center of the whole. However, Jesus knew that He was not only the master who represented everything on earth but also had to govern the spiritual realm, and because all these facts were obscured, He lived a life of even greater sorrow.

The responsibility for causing Jesus to abandon His life lies not only with the ancient people of Israel and the Jewish denominations but also with the household of Joseph and with Jesus' beloved disciples. 

So what should you, who understand these facts, do today? You must become a being who can comfort the returning Jesus, the hope of all people, on behalf of the nation, on behalf of many denominations, on behalf of countless families today, and on behalf of Jesus' beloved disciples.

Moreover, you must understand that God desires to see a being who is struggling to feel the sorrowful heart that Jesus felt deeply in His bones and flesh during His life, and that He has been working on this earth until now and is also working through the Holy Spirit.

The Saints of the Last Days Who Must Become Jesus' Representatives

Jesus went everywhere to preach the new gospel, facing disbelief and persecution wherever He moved, while taking on the worries and difficult problems of the nation of Israel. However, among the people at that time, there was not a single person who regarded the work and words of Jesus, who alone took on the worries of all humanity, as their own work and words. Therefore, today, you must resolve all the wrongs and sins of the Jewish people who rejected Jesus' words, the world that rejected Him, and the work of Jesus, and you must establish the ideals of Jesus on this earth. You must also seek to establish the ideals that Jesus sought to become a friend of all beings on behalf of the heavenly will.

Now, when we look at this from the perspective of the Bible, how much of Jesus' words did He manifest when He came to this earth? Jesus could not reveal the entire eternal ideal of God due to the disbelief of the Jewish people at that time. So what was that ideal of Jesus? His ideal was to unite heaven and earth to form one nation, one world, and one ideal garden. However, we must understand that this is not an easy task. 

When there is a nation, there is a national ideology. Additionally, there must be some political apparatus to govern that nation, which must have certain policies and, furthermore, a political party that establishes those policies. Thus, we can see that all citizens live around a certain political party. To establish a nation as a nation, it must go through this complex process to achieve its original purpose, and furthermore, each individual who must fulfill the great task of heavenly principles has the responsibility to seek and establish the words, life, and work of Jesus.

However, because no one has yet fulfilled that responsibility, the ideals of Jesus have not yet been realized on this earth, and you must understand that this has caused great sorrow before God. Also, you must become someone who emulates the faithfulness that Jesus showed in establishing the ideals of heaven.

The most important words Jesus spoke to His beloved disciples were, "You are my bride." In other words, Jesus came to this earth to establish the ideals of the bride and bridegroom. Therefore, today, you must advance to the position where, after passing through the positions of bride and bridegroom, you transcend family, society, and nation, and reach the place where you can unite with the ideals of the Creator, who is the Father representing heavenly principles. 

If there are shortcomings in the process you are advancing, you must clearly understand that you will cause Jesus a corresponding amount of sorrow. 

So what should the saints who find themselves in the end times do today? They must restore the words that can connect with Jesus' heart, restore the ideals of life, and restore His work. Thus, you must become someone who can transcend family, connect with society, nation, and the entire universe. 

Jesus was the one who had to establish the ideals of heaven, and because God wanted to establish Jesus as the Lord of the heavenly world, Jesus introduced a new ideology that could build heaven on this earth.

92   Let us become the brides who seek to restore what Jesus had lost. In order to take on such a mission, Jesus had to shake off all paths of His own life and walk a path that could represent a denomination and God. Thus, He walked a lonely path and left behind words of lament and desire for humanity, a fact that you must not forget today.

Living the Life of Practicing Jesus' Words

So what must you, who find yourselves in the end times, seek first in order to restore Jesus' work and build heaven on this earth? You must first seek the words that are the ideals of Jesus. You must establish the ideals of Jesus through your life. You must now find and practice the work of Jesus that is being rejected in your daily life. 

Thus, through the individual, passing through the form of family, through the form of denomination, advancing to the nation and the world, you must establish a relationship where when God moves, Jesus moves, and when Jesus moves, the earth can move. This kind of relationship cannot be established solely by the power of Jesus and the Holy Spirit. Therefore, the words of Jesus are words that can guard against the suffering in an evil world, that is, in an environment invaded by Satan.

So what must you understand now? You must understand that Jesus came to this earth and could not say all the words He had for all people, and that He did not complete His life and could not command all people after doing what He had to do. You must become someone who can feel the inner sorrow that caused Jesus to leave without accomplishing everything during His time on earth, in order to qualify as Jesus' bride.

A bride who receives the bridegroom must make the bridegroom's hopes her own hopes, and the bridegroom's life must become her own life, and the words of the bridegroom must become her own words, and the work of the bridegroom must become her own work, establishing an eternal relationship of oneness.
93 Just as you must go out, today you must also step forward to qualify as the bride of Jesus. Therefore, you must feel and experience the path that Jesus walked in your daily life, and furthermore, you must convey Jesus' words and intentions to the crowds of disbelief. Additionally, as you come to understand how earnest Jesus was about God's will, and as you become one with Him, you must approach your brothers with greater humility. Only then will you be able to comprehend the religious figures who have walked the path that humanity must take, the true path of life. So, what does Jesus desire for the saints who find themselves at the end of days today? Jesus hopes that you will become a bride who can stand as His counterpart. But what kind of bride is this? She is not merely a bride who stays at home, nor is she one who remains only within the Jewish community. She is a bride who can represent the chosen nation of Israel and its state, as well as the world. Moreover, she is a bride who can represent heaven and earth, take responsibility for God's work, and discuss matters according to the laws of justice to fulfill God's will. Jesus is looking for such a bride. Now, you must reflect on how much you have qualified as the bride that Jesus desires while living your faith. Are you truly seeking Jesus' work in your life? Are you genuinely striving to practice Jesus' ideals? In other words, in your words and actions, are you making an effort to represent Jesus' words and deeds? You must reflect on this. Thus, your life should be related to the ideals of Jesus at that time and should be actions associated with Jesus' work at that time. You must also take on the internal sorrow of Jesus, who came to this earth, lost all of His ideals, and left, and you must be able to relieve that sorrow. It is essential to recognize that this mission has been given to each one of you.

94 You must clearly understand that you are to become the bride who seeks to restore what Jesus had lost. You must connect with the sorrowful heart of Jesus, who lived with the sorrow of not fulfilling God's will, and you must become a person of true courage who fights to overcome adversity, even if you become weary and overwhelmed in the struggle to fulfill heaven's will. You must be someone who stands as a vanguard before Satan, unafraid even of the death on the cross, but rather stepping on that cross to give glory to heaven, emulating the practical life of Jesus. Furthermore, you should not be satisfied merely by imitating Jesus' practical life; you should not be content with having won a battle against Satan on any given day. You must strive to reach a place where the universe is governed eternally by Jesus' ideals, where the glory of heaven can manifest as Jesus' glory or your glory. In other words, you should be satisfied by achieving a day when you can move heaven, touch Jesus, and bring joy to the Father, resulting in joy for the entire universe.

What, then, should we seek? First, we must find you as individuals who stand in for Jesus' four corners. Each of you must become the individual representations of the past 12 tribes, and you must clearly understand the relationship between the Christ who was established to represent the 12 tribes and those tribes. In any environment, you must become the protagonists of heaven who live and work to realize His ideals on this earth. Additionally, you must understand the sorrow of Jesus, who represented the family, and the circumstances that caused sorrow for the church, and you must unite among yourselves to take on the final mission. Furthermore, we must create a denomination that can represent Israel and Judaism at that time and become individuals who can fulfill all that the apostles were to accomplish before Satan on behalf of heaven. If the apostles at that time created individuals who could stand in for humanity, a nation that could stand in for all of Israel, and a world that could be created, what more could Jesus have said? Furthermore, since they failed to establish the laws that required them to unconditionally obey, submit, and practice Jesus' words, you must become individuals who can restore all of this today.

Now, when you realize that Jesus lived on this earth, fought on this earth, and drank on this earth, yet finished His life without finding any of the purposes He aimed for, it is not enough to simply follow the path Jesus walked. You must be able to feel the internal sorrow of the bridegroom, Jesus, who had no choice but to lead His beloved disciples down the path of death. You must also carry the historical mistakes that made the bridegroom lonely and led Him to the cross, while looking forward to a hopeful day and fighting on. In other words, you must realize Jesus' fundamental ideals, relieve the internal grievances He bore, and fulfill the work He left behind.

So, what should the saints at the end of days do? They must become beings who can resolve the grievances of God and Jesus that have accumulated over 6,000 years of history. Even if the path is the way of the cross and the thorny path, they must become heavenly warriors who are prepared to die and dedicate their lives to building God's kingdom on this earth. God established the nation of Israel over 4,000 years of history and promised to send the Messiah to them, but because the nation of Israel and the apostles were disbelieving, Jesus could not say all He wanted to say to the nation of Israel, nor could He fully express His words to His disciples. We must become people who understand that Jesus had such internal sorrow.

96 You must also recognize that the grievances of such sorrow still remain on this earth, and you should feel that they are still moving towards your hearts at this time. Moreover, you must not only take on the Satan that Jesus faced, but you must also be able to take responsibility for the countless lives on this earth today.

Desperate struggles against Satan that obstruct the path

So, where is the difficult problem in today's faith journey? The issue is whether you can establish any conditions to inherit the internal sorrow that Jesus could not reveal to humanity. Considering this, if you are to regain the lost words of Jesus at the end of days, you must have a firm resolution and determination to achieve God's will without falling, regardless of the trials and persecutions on this earth. Just as there were Satans who tried to kill Jesus and led Him to abandon His life, you must understand that similar environments will arise when you try to live on behalf of Jesus' will today. In other words, just as families, denominations, and nations abandoned Jesus' work at that time, similar circumstances will come upon you.

Those who sold Jesus to the enemy and handed Him over to the cross were none other than His disciples, and those who disbelieved and persecuted Him, not knowing that He was the Messiah chosen by God, were the nation of Israel. Furthermore, because such disbelief has caused grievances against God, the work of Satan has not ended until now. Therefore, in your faith journey today, you must recognize that the same things that caused the Lord Jesus to be abandoned, His words to be abandoned, and His work to be abandoned are appearing again. 

Thus, today Satan prevents you from transcending your personal limitations. The will of Jesus is to reach through you as individuals, through your families, and extend to society, the nation, and the world. However, Satan is blocking you from going beyond your personal limitations in your living environment. Therefore, when you find yourselves in a living environment similar to that of Jesus' time, you must be willing to risk your life and fight to break free from that environment.

When you try to represent Jesus' words and fight against Satan, you will inevitably encounter difficult circumstances that no one can understand. Furthermore, even if you find yourselves in such a position, you must establish some direct conditions that represent Jesus' life and overcome them.

Now, what should you, who have been looking at the ideals of the bride and living your faith, do? You must be able to fulfill the ideals of the entirety of Jesus' life, the ideals of universal hope, on behalf of Jesus. Only then can you be assured of stepping into the position of Jesus' bride. 

Today, where are you staying? You must not remain in an environment that is stuck in your individual lamentations. You must become someone who transcends such an environment. You must be able to follow in the footsteps of Jesus, who walked despite all opposition from beloved parents, beloved siblings, and loved ones. If you cannot do this, you will not be able to return to your original humanity, and the Unification Church will lose its value of existence.

If you understand that the providential work based on these principles is unfolding, then you must enter that path, and once you do, you must not strive to fulfill your personal desires, but rather work for the whole. You must find the words that can replace the lost words of Jesus and live a life that can replace the life of Jesus. Even if Jesus did not see the fulfillment of the promise of all authority in heaven and earth given to Him by God, He did not lose heart, and you must learn from such a character of Jesus.

Therefore, today you must reflect on whether you have become a bride who can always welcome the bridegroom, Jesus, by following in His footsteps, and consider what kind of environment you are living in and what mountains you are overcoming. Thus, after crossing the bloody path that the saints must take, you must be ready to welcome the Lord who will return in glory.

The glory of the Lord that you will meet after crossing the peak of suffering

So, when the returning Lord appears in the glory of God, what should you do? If you are to welcome the returning Lord, that joy must not end with you as an individual. It must manifest as joy that represents eternity or the infinite ideals of heaven. In other words, even if you feel temporary joy, do not be satisfied with it; rather, you must feel the eternal joy of having fought and won against Satan, experiencing God's eternal love. Additionally, in experiencing grace, you must feel the extraordinary grace that Jesus felt, which is beyond imagination.

How did Jesus come to feel such grace? It was because He cut off all matters in His life and focused solely on God's will. What allowed Jesus to behold the glory of resurrection? It was because He could remain unchanged and serve God, even if all the glories of heaven and earth and the ideals that no human on earth could possess were severed. Thus, Jesus entered directly into the realm of God's glory and stood in a position to relate to humanity on this earth.

So, what is the joy that you feel today? That joy is never for your own sake. It is a grace that empowers you to fight against the forces of Satan on this earth. Therefore, you must express your gratitude to the Father who has given you joy, and after winning the battle against Satan, you must raise a joyful song of victory that has removed the grievances accumulated over 6,000 years on this earth, rejoicing forever in unity with the Father.

Thus, the grace you have received is not a grace that will lead you forever, nor is it a grace for your own sake. It is a grace that compels you to fight against Satan and to subdue him. Therefore, you must not establish any conditions of comfort for yourself with the grace you have received, but rather you must remove all sin and the forces of Satan on this earth. When you appear as victorious sons and daughters who have fulfilled God's purpose of creation on this earth, or as those who have met all conditions for restoration, Satan will be of no use, no matter how much he struggles. Furthermore, if there is someone who appears in such a manner, they will be free wherever they go, and there will always be traces of victory in their footsteps.

So, do you feel something as you listen to this message today? Have you gained new insights or found something? Or have you learned something through the principles after entering the Unification Church? If that is the truth, you must not only understand it with your head. You must understand it with your heart, and as you understand it with your heart, you must also embody it, and as you embody it, you must also grasp it with your spirit.
100   Let us become brides who find and establish what Jesus had cast away. When you come to know this in your heart, you will have no choice but to move in order to achieve the purpose of that word, and you will have no choice but to fight against Satan. Even if you want to open your mouth to curse the Father and turn your thoughts to betray heaven, you will find that you cannot do so. As pioneers of Shincheonji who fulfill their responsibilities and move forward to the end, when you come to know the word with your head, heart, body, and mind, you will feel the countless arrows of Satan coming from around you. The more you feel it, the more you will have no choice but to unite with those who are in the same position as you. You must understand that such a person is a pioneer of Shincheonji. In this way, you must show the gifts you have received through your daily life in practical fields, and you must have the heart to overcome and block any arrows or accusations from Satan. Until today, you have not been able to create an environment on this earth where you can live intoxicated by the glory of heaven. Therefore, until now, God and the angels have been cooperating behind the scenes to lead humanity on earth toward that glorious gift, and you must understand that God is still in sorrow.

101 Jesus had this sorrowful heart of God, and with a new law of heaven, He tried to establish an eternal ideological relationship with humanity on earth as a condition, but due to the disbelief of the people at that time, He could not fulfill that purpose and sadly and unjustly died on the cross. If you establish the condition that you have fulfilled the purpose of representing the will of Jesus on this earth, the Satan who caused the fall of the human ancestors, Adam and Eve, will naturally disappear from this earth. Therefore, you must understand that once humanity overcomes just one peak in the battle against Satan on this earth, heaven will always be with them. 102   You must remember that you will be able to restore all that was lost and stand as one who understands all the sorrows He endured, or as one who possesses the value of victory. <Prayer> Father! 6) Let us occupy the glorious new nation
1 Thessalonians 5:1-11 If humanity had not fallen, the garden of hope called the 'glorious new nation' would have been a world that we should joyfully welcome within our living sphere today, but due to the fall of humanity, you all know well that we are unable to connect with that garden of hope today. You must once again think about the responsibility and duty we have to build this glorious new nation, even if it means sacrificing all we have with all our might and sincerity. If humanity had been centered on God and had achieved completion, the joy of humanity would have been God's joy, and the glory enjoyed by humanity would have been God's glory. However, because humanity could not enjoy its own joy and glory based on what God desires, sorrow began for humanity. And because humanity has sinned, it has fallen far from the garden of that ideal. You all know well that the historical effort to find these fallen humans is the work of restoration providence. So, what kind of garden is that providential garden? It is a place where all created beings, centered on the Creator, live enjoying unified glory within the ideological realm of their Creator. It was a garden with such a purpose, but due to the fall of humanity, we have become unable to sing the glory of God in a unified position where we can have the ideology of unity. Therefore, we must understand that God has been working through a long historical process to establish a unified ideology of unity. 

The struggle of humanity to build the glorious new nation
When we look at ourselves as humans, we must unite our hearts and bodies, and based on that united self, all of humanity must become one, and from the position of united humanity, we have the responsibility to create a unified operation law and operation rate of nature. Furthermore, we have a significant responsibility to create a unified operation law and operation rate of the heavenly principles. To achieve the glorious new ideology and build the glorious new nation, we must unify our bodies with our hearts. And centered on ourselves, all of humanity must be unified, and at the same time, we must become one with the operation laws of all heaven and earth, and furthermore, we must unite with the heavenly principles that the Creator has been working out. Otherwise, God's glory cannot be manifested on this earth, that is, in the created world. You must understand that if God's glory does not manifest, we cannot even think of such a thing as the glorious new nation. 

In order to build this glorious new nation, we must consider what historical process humanity has gone through. We can see that it has gone through an endless history of struggle for a long time. We are in a position where we must unite with the operation laws of all nature below us and align with the laws of heaven above us. Thus, we have the dual responsibility to align with both the operation laws of nature and the laws of heavenly principles through the historical process of struggle. You must not forget that our ancestors have worked hard to fulfill these responsibilities.

105 You must understand that throughout all historical development processes, such as when clan society developed into tribal society, there was always darkness blocking the way. Just as we can only maintain life on the foundation of victory over all the powers of death that come upon us, you must understand that there were always forces of darkness, that is, opposing forces, blocking the advancement from clan to tribe and from tribe to nation. So what does God advocate and govern? The fall means losing unity. The heart and body have been divided, all the operation laws of nature and the laws of heavenly principles and the entire ideology have been divided, and ten million people have all been divided. You must understand that heaven has been working through history, establishing something unified centered on tribes or nations to gather this all together. Therefore, clan society becomes tribal society, several tribal societies gather to form nations and states, and several states form alliances. What comes next is unification. Unification means converging any ideology or principle into one to form a unified ideological realm. This is how the order of the universe was meant to be maintained. You must align the operation laws of this moving created world with your heart, and at the same time, you must establish a relationship with the ideology and laws that the Creator desires. Otherwise, you cannot become the ultimate victor, nor can you possess the highest human qualities that enable you to govern all creation on behalf of the glory of all things. God has gathered numerous tribes to create tribes, integrated tribes to create nations, and united nations to bring about one world, and this providence culminates in the one man and one woman that God established at the time of creation. In other words, you must understand that God has been working through the restoration providence to build the glorious new nation that He intended to grant to humanity from the beginning.

106   Let us occupy the glorious new nation
So what is our lament? It is that we do not have an environment where everything can be concentrated around one person, and we cannot stand as beings who can concentrate the surrounding environment. What has caused this? It is the forces of darkness that have created this situation. Even if there is a heart that aims for goodness in every corner, because this heart could not connect with each other, there are high lights that can be a light to a clan or nation, which are like the morning light and the evening light, and these beings are undergoing the historical process of struggle through the night period. 

Religion and science aiming for dual unity
Today, many apostles are saying that this time is the end. Today, there are two camps: democracy and communism, one of which can replace the morning and the other can replace the evening. You must understand that there is something blocking between these two camps, and you must take on the mission to break through this. The world is in a chaotic state where everything is confused, unable to find a center or direction, and the responsibility to resolve this chaos does not lie with God, nor with nature, but with us humans. Because God has placed the responsibility on humanity to achieve a comprehensive unifying ideology, humans are developing natural science that studies nature into a form of unified science, and they are unifying the world of the heart through religion. In the late 16th century, religion and science were separated, but in today's end times, we are transitioning back to a stage of unification that can achieve one purpose. Here, science is taking the form of unity first, and this is because, until Adam was created as a perfect person, the body was first made and then the spirit was breathed into it, which is the principle of creation. You must also have a humble heart that recognizes that the material you are to give should not be taken for yourself. Only then can the nature hidden in your heart be manifested, and you can enter into the realm of eternal hope, which is why you must understand that Jesus spoke about the attitude toward using material things. So now, what is it that you must treat as an enemy? It is the selfishness that thinks the material given to you is for your own benefit. Therefore, if you have even a piece of bread, you should be able to represent God's heart, which desires that all people share it. If you have something to eat, you should have the heart to give it to your family before you eat it, and you should have the heart to give it to society, the nation, and all of humanity. Only by possessing such a heart can a person complete their journey through normal processes, but most people today live forgetting this. You should feel sorry for this and recognize that it is also a position of fall. So, how does the enemy come in today? It comes through material conditions. However, God's blessings also come through material things. You must clearly understand that both God and our enemy come through material things, and you must become a person who can establish a firm center of faith through material things.

128 When you establish a center, relative existences naturally arise there. Since a perfect plus naturally generates a perfect minus, it is a principle of the universe that you must find and establish a principled center of faith, a standard on this earth. You must clearly understand that Jesus called out to seek first the kingdom and His righteousness because He knew such principles. What else must you understand? You must understand that fights arise among family members over food. Fights break out between mothers-in-law and daughters-in-law, brothers and sisters, and nations fight among themselves over food. You must understand that this is why Jesus lived with a painful heart for the family, society, nation, and world, wishing to rise above such issues and expressing His sorrow for not being able to build the kingdom and His righteousness. Therefore, today you must also empathize with Jesus' heart and strive to resemble His character. Next, fights will arise over clothing before you. There will be a process in your faith journey that you must resolve regarding clothing. Therefore, today you must be able to resolve such issues freely without being affected by any accusations from Satan. In this way, you must understand that your issues of eating and wearing become Satan while also becoming the practical field where Satan can operate. Therefore, you must be aware that everything you do is something Satan is trying to invade, and you must become someone who does not present any conditions for Satan to invade. Thus, today you must not live only for yourself. You must live for a greater purpose. If you belong to a family, living for that family will become living for yourself.
129 Yes, when you belong to one nation and live for that nation, it also becomes living for yourself. Likewise, when you live for heaven, you truly find yourself living for yourself. Therefore, today you must keep in mind that all these facts are being realized and manifested through your living environment. If you have food, you should also have the heart to give it to those who persecute you. At such times, you will be able to feel the heart of Paul when he lamented, “Oh, wretched man that I am!” (Romans 7:24). Many prophets and sages who came to become such protagonists have been buried, persecuted, and mocked throughout history. Therefore, today, God's hope for you is to establish a self that can resolve all historical wrongs. Now, what must you do to fulfill God's hopeful will? First, you must become a person who follows Jesus Christ, who walked the path of the cross, shedding blood for the kingdom of God and its righteousness, and next, you must follow the path that countless prophets and sages have taken over the past 6000 years, who have forsaken their own glory to fulfill God's will. However, if you do not take such a path and instead walk a path for your own glory, you will not be able to stand before God or before the countless prophets and sages with dignity. Furthermore, even after death, you will not be able to stand before the Father or be embraced in the arms of His love. In other words, those who believe for themselves and die only to gain salvation for themselves will not be able to stand before the Father with dignity in the afterlife. 

The people who seek to establish that nation and its righteousness must therefore deny themselves and live for that nation and its righteousness.
