A person who denies themselves and serves society, the nation, and the world is the one who can build God's kingdom. Furthermore, a person who can build heaven is one who, even if they deny the nation and the world, lives for heaven. Matthew 10:16-42 <Prayer> Father, who has labored to awaken us even in times of difficulty! We first thank you for allowing us to seek you and bow before you even amidst the harsh powers of Satan that stretch over this rugged earth. The fact that we are here today is due to your labor, and we ask that you allow us to feel once again that being able to claim we are your sons and daughters is the result of your infinite love. Father, we have gathered this evening to hear your words, and we earnestly hope and wish that you may reveal your words of counsel to your beloved sons and daughters at this time. Today, this earth is in a position similar to that of the 600,000 people of ancient Israel who, after 40 years of wandering in the wilderness, failed to follow Joshua and Caleb, who had resolved to face the promised land of Canaan. Father, we ask that you counsel us on this, and also allow us to remember that the words emphasized by heaven to Joshua and Caleb at that time, “Be strong and courageous,” are words we must hold in our hearts today. Beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Countless Satans may be trying to sweep us away with harsh trials and severe persecutions, blocking our path with the cross, but we ask that you allow us to become proud sons and daughters who can establish the will of heaven with unwavering loyalty. At this time, may we take one step closer to you and be able to say, “The mountain offering we can give to you is our bodies and hearts, so please accept us.” We earnestly hope and wish for this, beloved Father. Father, we know that you are concerned for us even at this hour. Father, please do not let even one of us enter into the darkness, and we know that the time is approaching when we must sing of the glory of your joy. Therefore, we ask that today we may not be unable to take the path we should go because we are worried about our own affairs, and that we may not lack in experiencing the hearts of the countless prophets and sages who have gone before us and the heart of heaven. Beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Father, now in this hour, we wish to repent for the shortcomings of our past lives and go forth with new resolutions and determination. Please allow us to be sons and daughters who can reach out toward your infinite love. Beloved Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. We ask that the remaining time be solely under your guidance, and that it may not become a time for Satan to take advantage. We earnestly hope for your protection with the grace of glory and for your loving hands to embrace us. We pray all these things in the name of the Lord. On the other hand, when sending out the disciples to deliver the new gospel to the chosen nation of Israel, we must understand that the feelings and circumstances of the departing disciples were pitiful, but so were the feelings and circumstances of Jesus, who was sending them, a situation that no one could express. Furthermore, you must understand that Jesus, knowing that the disciples would have to fight against countless Satans, wished for them to win and sing of the Father's glory, and He spoke these words with concern that they might stumble along the way and cause worry in heaven. The heart of Jesus, who sent out the disciples for evangelism, was that of a loving master who hoped that His beloved disciples would step forward with a final resolution for the fight, knowing that enemies would surely appear, and He wished for them to win and enjoy the joy of proving that they are the sons and daughters of the Father. You must not regard these words as being meant only for the apostles of that time. God's Double Sorrow
Then what kind of sorrow does God have? This is an extremely important issue that we must understand. It is the sorrow that arose because Adam and Eve, who were to be the central responsible figures for fulfilling the ideal of creation, fell and failed to establish the original world of creation that they were to build through them. Therefore, today you must become someone who can feel such sorrow of God. In other words, because Adam and Eve fell, the ideal of creation that was to allow them to enjoy eternal happiness centered on God's eternal love and ideals was frustrated, and God has had to toil throughout thousands of years of history until now. Therefore, today you must become someone who can feel the sorrowful heart that God has felt while fighting against Satan to achieve the ideal of creation that Adam and Eve could not fulfill. Now, you must feel the sorrow of God when He lost Adam, the sorrow of God when Adam and Eve betrayed Him and fell. To do this, you must first understand what God's love is and how much God loves humanity. If you do not do this, you will have no way to feel the heart of God who mourned over losing Adam and Eve. Therefore, today you must first feel the sorrowful heart of God who could not fulfill the ideal of creation due to the fall of Adam and Eve. The heart of God, who is in anguish to fulfill the ideal of creation, is bound up in all of creation. You must understand that the history of providence until now has been to overcome that. What did all the prophets and sages who came from Noah to Abraham, Moses, and Jesus testify to humanity on this earth? They simply conveyed God's sorrow to ignorant humans. You must understand that God has been filled with sorrow because He could not fulfill the ideal of creation due to the fall of humanity, and that He has sent numerous prophets and sages to fulfill that ideal and has had to watch them fight against Satan and feel sorrow. In other words, the numerous prophets and sages have walked the painful path of labor to introduce God's will and His sorrowful heart, which no one has welcomed until now, to the ignorant people who have betrayed God. The more the sorrowful heart of God is felt internally, the more they felt the mission to mourn on behalf of the earth, and they had to fight against Satan with a heart similar to God's sorrowful heart. They were to appear as beings recognized for their value on behalf of God's eternal will, yet they were despised and rejected by ignorant humans, and as they were pushed around without value, God felt double sorrow as He looked upon them. For God, the sorrow of not being able to fulfill His ideal of creation is one sorrow, but it is another indescribable sorrow to see the numerous prophets and sages who are destined to awaken ignorant humans on the earth and fight against Satan. You must not forget that God has had this double sorrow. Looking back at the time of Noah, for 1600 years, God was filled with indescribable sorrow but walked the path of patience. Even though the sorrow for humanity was overwhelming and could not be forgotten for a single moment, He chose Noah to fully express His sorrow before all people or all creation.

Let us become those who know God's sorrow
Then why did God place Noah in a position that humans at that time could not understand? For 1600 years, as humanity caused God to be filled with sorrow, He established Noah to allow him to feel that heavenly sorrow and sadness on behalf of humanity, and you must understand that He placed him in such an incomprehensible environment. Noah appeared silently before those who disbelieved and opposed him for 120 years. Even when he received the warning from heaven that the earth would be judged after 120 years, he fulfilled his duty of faith toward heaven. He was called a righteous man because he was righteous, and the more the society he lived in became corrupt, the more he worried and mourned for that society. While many people were struggling to secure their own comfort, only Noah struggled to seek the laws of justice, worried about the heavenly principles, and mourned in an environment that others did not want. You must understand that it was because of Noah, who had a heart to worry and mourn for humanity at that time, that God called him. It was not only Noah. What was the reason that all the prophets and sages who have had the responsibility to fulfill God's will until now were chosen? It was because they alone worried about the corrupt land and corrupt humanity of their time. With such a heart that cares for individuals, families, societies, nations, and the world, they prayed with a sorrowful heart toward heaven, saying, "Is there heaven? If so, please save this land of sin." Because they devoted themselves with a sorrowful heart toward heaven, they were able to receive the call from heaven. You must understand that when God chose Noah or any prophet, His heart was filled with indescribable sorrow. Furthermore, when the prophets called by God were met with disbelief and betrayal from humanity on earth, and they cried out with a sorrowful heart, "Oh! Father!" their cries were not sounds of joy for humanity. However, when God heard such prayers, He was moved by their earnest appeals, which is why until today, many prophets and sages have walked the path of suffering to comfort God's sorrow, regardless of the hardships they faced. Anyone who has a sorrowful heart and appeals and prays to heaven in this way has caused God to feel an even greater sorrowful heart toward them. You must understand that when God faced them, His heart was moved to seek all His desires and ideals. However, God was always in a position where He could not command His beloved prophets or beloved sons and daughters with peace of mind, and it was a situation where He could not discuss matters beyond time and place. You must understand God's sorrow, which could only face humanity after establishing such symbolic conditions. Thus, in the Old Testament era, God worked to remove His sorrow through offerings, and in the New Testament era, He worked through Jesus. However, that does not mean that God's will has been fully accomplished. God wants to directly exchange hearts with you, embrace you, and live together with you forever within the realm of His love. He wants to call all humanity His sons and daughters. You must understand that He has endured until today, wanting to express all His grievances and sorrowful feelings. Today, you who live on this earth may express your sorrow to people, to your family, or to your race, but God cannot do so. You may express your circumstances by saying, "I am sad, or I am lonely," during difficult times, but even through the thousands of years of historical processes, God has not been able to say a single word of sorrow. You must be able to feel God's heart in such a sorrowful position.
172   Let us become those who know God's sorrowUntil now, the prophets and sages of history have expressed their own sorrows only after first revealing the sorrows of all humanity on earth in their stead. If you wish to stand before heaven now, you must first reflect on your past. You should recall whether you have done even the smallest thing that could bring comfort to God, who has been sorrowful for 6000 long years within your sphere of life. 

Humans must relieve God's sorrowThus, you must become someone who looks to the future, someone who is concerned for your family, this nation, and this people. Even if the world is shaken and swept away into the realm of death, you must become someone who walks toward heaven with an unchanging heart. If you become such a person, you will never perish, and you will not be cursed by God. 

For this reason, God is sorrowful because humanity has fallen and has not fulfilled the ideal of creation, and He is searching for someone who will worry and work on behalf of this earth to achieve that unfulfilled ideal. Today, you are in a position where you must comfort God, who is in such a sorrowful state, and find a way to remove that sorrow. 

However, you do not fully understand that it is humanity that has caused sorrow to God, and therefore it is also humanity that must expel that sorrow. You must realize that you yourself are the one who must relieve God's sorrow and strive to do so. This is the greatest issue that you must take seriously. 

Until now, God has never had a moment in the lives of the chosen humans where He was not sorrowful. This is because, while there are those who fulfill their central mission with all their heart to relieve God's sorrow, He has had to see that, at no moment, has His heart been comforted to the extent He desires. God has been in a position where He has shared His heart with the humans He has chosen, but they have not been able to fulfill His hopes during their time, which has caused Him great distress. 

After 4000 years of this sorrowful history, God finally sent one being who could replace the 4000 years of history on this earth, who could stand in for all the prophets who came and went during those 4000 years, and who could represent all of creation. The being who could stand in for heaven, all things, and humanity is none other than Jesus Christ, whom you believe in. You must understand that the day He came was a day when all things could rejoice, a day when all people could rejoice, and a day when heaven could rejoice. 

So what did Jesus bring to this earth? He came as the being who could replace the sorrows of all humanity in the historical process, the being who bore unspeakable sorrow. He came with the responsibility to relieve the sorrows that had been pent up in God's heart for 4000 years on behalf of all humanity and all creation. 

Jesus fought against Satan, who was blocking the lives of humanity and the universe, in order to reverse the history of humanity's fall, which had resulted from humanity's betrayal of God. He pursued an ideology, a hope, and a joy that was in relationship with God, without being connected to any satanic lineage. 

Although Jesus walked this path for over 30 years, not a single person believed in Him or sympathized with Him. He devoted over 30 years of blood, sweat, and tears to relieve God's sorrow and fulfill His will, yet there was no one who truly understood His circumstances. He was driven out by the Jewish community and the people of Israel, and eventually had no place to stay, wandering from town to town and from mountain to mountain, and you must feel the sorrowful circumstances of Jesus today. 

173   Let us become those who know God's sorrowSo what was Jesus' sorrow? It was the sorrow of not being able to fulfill His mission before God's will, and the sorrow of not being able to awaken the ignorant people to God's will. Therefore, Jesus was sorrowful towards the Judaism that opposed and disbelieved in Him at that time, and He was sorrowful towards the nation of Israel. 

God, who looked upon Jesus in such a sorrowful situation, wanted to immediately judge and destroy the Judaism and the nation of Israel that persecuted and disbelieved in Him, but He could not do so. You must understand that there was this painful sorrow in God. 

Jesus came to this earth as the Savior of all people and was sorrowful because He replaced the sorrows of all humanity and all creation. Therefore, you must now take on the heart to penetrate Jesus' lonely heart and feel what His sorrow was like. You must have the desire to become a friend of Jesus Christ, who was in a sorrowful position that no one knew about. Even if you cannot be a friend of Jesus for a day, you should at least aspire to be a friend for an hour. If you do not have even a little of that heart, you will not be able to step forward on behalf of heaven, nor will you be able to comfort God's sorrow on behalf of humanity, and instead, you will find yourself in the position of a rebel against heaven. 

You must be able to feel God's sorrowful heart as you look upon Jesus, who worked tirelessly to fulfill His mission, only to ultimately be crucified. Jesus had the mission to relieve God's sorrow on behalf of all humanity and the universe, and to fulfill God's will by overcoming Satan, but He was driven here and there by the disbelieving crowd and ultimately had to bear the cross on Golgotha. What must have been Jesus' heart in such a situation? 

He felt that all the promises made around Him were destroyed and that His life ultimately culminated in the cross, yet He did not betray heaven until the end and fulfilled His duty of loyalty to heaven. Although all humans disbelieved in Jesus, He did not let that affect Him and made the path toward heaven the goal of His life. You must remember that Jesus' life has historically become a path of hope for us humans. 

Just before His death on the cross, He prayed, "My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?" (Matthew 26:46), and you must be able to understand God's painful and sorrowful heart as He looked upon Jesus in that position. God has endured sorrow for 4000 years, but because He cannot directly govern until His beloved sons and daughters establish some condition of indemnity, He has no choice but to wait until they establish that condition. 

So how did Jesus live on this earth? Did He speak and act freely like you do today? No, He could not. Jesus was always in a position of hardship. No matter where He slept, what He ate, or where He moved, He could not help but express the sorrowful heart of God. Wherever He spoke, He felt as if His bones were melting and His blood and flesh were withering away due to the sorrows inflicted upon Him by the disbelieving crowd, and He cried out loudly before the Pharisees, the Jews, and the nation of Israel. 

Jesus could not discuss the various sorrows he suffered from them with the ignorant people and the disbelieving crowd, as He bore the deep resentment from those sorrows. You must not forget today that there was such a painful situation for Jesus. 

Knowing the mission He received from heaven to come to this earth, Jesus could not help but feel sorrowful because the hope of heaven and the reality in which He lived were so far apart. The sorrow that Jesus sought to know God's sorrow could cover heaven and earth, but He could not bear the sorrow arising from His own circumstances. 

Today, you must also follow the life of Jesus, who did not become entangled in His own circumstances but instead worried about and sought to comfort the sorrows of all humanity and the historical sorrows of God during His 30 years of life. You must reflect on how much you have worried about Jesus' sorrowful circumstances and how far you have advanced toward that sorrowful position to fulfill God's will. 

The sorrow of God has increased due to Jesus being crucifiedWhen Adam and Eve fell, God felt an indescribable sorrow because He lost the ideal of creation. Therefore, God wanted to have a day of hope where humans would believe in Jesus and comfort His sorrowful heart, but He once again witnessed the miserable situation of Jesus being crucified. After 4000 years of effort to establish Jesus to relieve His sorrow and build the kingdom of heaven on this earth, what must have been God's heart when all of that will was frustrated at once? 

At that moment, God's sorrow was greater than the sorrow He felt when Adam and Eve fell. When Adam and Eve fell, He felt a sorrow as if heaven and earth were collapsing, but when Jesus died on the cross, it was as if the tower of devotion built with blood, sweat, and tears over 4000 years collapsed all at once, forcing God to begin the history of re-creation again. Thus, God could not help but feel an indescribable sorrow, compounded by the sorrow of the fall. 

So what position are you in today? Today, you are the descendants of Adam and Eve, who brought sorrow to God through their fall. You must also understand that you are the descendants of those who increased God's sorrow by killing Jesus, who came to relieve God's sorrow. 

God has not forgotten that humanity has betrayed Him by bringing Him sorrow, and He continues to guide the descendants. God is eagerly awaiting the day when all creation will become one and His kingdom will be established on this earth. 

So what kind of environment are you living in now? What is the reality you are looking at today? What situation is the world in? If you are a person of purpose, it is time to look at today's reality and beat your chest, weeping and sorrowful. If there is someone who knows the mission of Jesus Christ, who came to introduce God's love to this earth and comfort God's sorrowful heart, he cannot help but strike his own dark and dull heart on behalf of the whole earth. This is because today's reality is so far from God's will and is filled with immorality, contradictions, and struggles. 

Therefore, today you must feel God's deeply sorrowful heart and yearn for His infinite love, regardless of whether others insult or persecute you. You must strive to establish the kingdom of God on this earth, even if it means struggling and collapsing in the process. This is the historical responsibility that lies upon us. 

You must not bring your own sad circumstances to God, who is in a position of even greater sorrow than you, even if you have various sad stories from the disbelief you suffer from. God's sorrow toward humanity is immeasurable, but He has never shown it entirely before humanity until now. 

Today, just as God has carried His sorrow while working for the salvation of humanity, you must also carry your own sorrow and fight against Satan. When you pray, you should forget all about yourself and become someone who resolves the Father's sorrow, praying to take on all the historical resentment and cosmic sorrow that has been pent up in the Father until now. And you must fight against Satan to fulfill God's will. 

If you become such a person, you will never perish, even if you struggle and disappear while trying to fulfill God's will. For this reason, God is still hoping for such a person to appear at this time. He is searching for someone who wants to relieve the Father's sorrow, even if it means sacrificing their own life. God wants to infuse that person with the infinite life force of heaven's providence, relieve His sorrow through them, and establish an eternal relationship with them. He also wants to resolve familial sorrows, social sorrows, national sorrows, and even global sorrows through them, and you must understand this clearly at this time. 

God's desire for humanitySo what kind of deep sorrow does heaven have for you? You should not have sorrow for yourself. If you have sorrow for yourself, you are an unhappy person. You must have sorrow for your family, society, nation, world, and even God, and become someone who resolves all those sorrows. 

Recall the old man Noah. When God warned that He would judge this earth with a flood 120 years later, Noah believed that warning and did not forget it for a single moment over those 120 years. He obeyed that one command for 120 years. This is an astonishing faith. However, Noah was not the only one who absolutely obeyed God's word. Abraham was also someone who absolutely obeyed God's word. When God told him to leave Ur of the Chaldeans, Abraham never forgot that word of blessing even when he was in the wilderness. Thus, Abraham believed in the promise of that blessing and fought against Satan every day. 

Jacob was also such a person. Because he did not forget the blessings he received from Isaac and God, he was able to endure 21 years of hard labor in Haran. Jesus was also such a person. Jesus, too, received a single command given to Him as a promise and fought against Satan for over 30 years to fulfill that promise. 

You must understand that all the prophets called before God have uniformly kept the one word given to them from heaven with their entire lives in faith. 

So what should you do in this era where historical sorrow is passing through you? First, you must become someone who experiences God's sorrow, and you must also become someone who experiences the feelings of Jesus and the Holy Spirit, who have sorrow for God and humanity, as well as the feelings of the many prophets and sages who have come and gone over the past 6000 years. Thus, you must become someone who casts aside everything and resolves all historical sorrows, giving joy and glory to God. You must not forget that God is earnestly hoping for such a person even at this time.

<Prayer> As we think about the historical battles that must be fought to inherit Your legacy even after death, we present ourselves before You, Father. When we consider the responsibility and mission we have to subdue this tremendous enemy before You, we realize that we have sought a life of ease and have been too immersed in grace, wanting only to receive Your love. Father, please forgive us. 

We have forgotten that to subdue our enemies, we must remain steadfast in spirit and heart, even amidst fierce storms, battles, and the adversities of the cross. From now on, allow us to hold onto an unchanging heart and become heavenly soldiers who can fight alone against countless Satans. We earnestly desire this, beloved Father. 

In carrying out this mission, are there sons and daughters who are weary from the fight? Father, grant them strength. Are there those who hesitate? Please give them courage. So that they may run towards the goal of victory and charge straight towards the objective of the battle, allow them to be beloved sons and daughters, we earnestly ask, beloved Father. 

We have the responsibility to cross over the hill of Golgotha to victory after the final confrontation, so may we run towards all these battlefields with Your strength, heart, determination, and resolve, and become Your sons and daughters who can win with deep-seated grievances. We earnestly desire this, beloved Father. 

Though the gathered sons and daughters are few in number, do not allow them to be satisfied with where they are, and let them know how to be grateful for the gifts given. May they understand that the gifts given today are not for themselves alone, but represent the responsibility and mission to subdue millions of Satans on behalf of all humanity, both on earth and among the countless saints in heaven. We earnestly desire this, beloved Father.

So that they may be sons and daughters who can fight alone, bearing the responsibility for Your will, Your gifts, and Your providence without faltering, we earnestly desire this, beloved Father.

<Word> If there had been no providence of restoration from God since the fall until today, humanity, which is bound to sin, would not have been able to dare to call You 'Father' through their mouths, nor could they think of You as the heavenly gift or the gift of love in the form of death. 

Moreover, we must understand that the reason we remain in the realm of life today is due to the grace of God, who has tirelessly continued the work of restoration. 

God, who sought to embrace humanity through Jesus, has the entirety of His providential life encapsulated within it. The providence of God passed through 4000 years of history until the sending of Jesus, and through Jesus’ coming to this earth, God was able to initiate a new providence centered on Him. 

In other words, because God could not freely interact with earthly humans, He had sent numerous angels to carry out His providence during the Old Testament era. By establishing Christ, who has a substantial form to directly work on earth, He was able to start the providence to embrace fallen humanity once again. This is the significance of the birth of Christ that you must understand. 

Since Christ came and left, 2000 years of history have passed. Therefore, today, you must realize that by entering into the realm of Your gifts, you can acknowledge Jesus Christ as your Lord and receive grace under the protection of the Holy Spirit. 

You must understand that during the 4000 years before Jesus came, there was a providence of God who could not directly engage with humanity, sending numerous angels to find them. You must also recognize that God, who separated the spiritual and physical realms, sent Jesus Christ to establish a direct and flat providence before humanity. 

Today, as 2000 years have passed since Jesus Christ came and left, you must experience the heart of God who sought humanity spiritually during the 4000 years before Jesus. 

Moreover, when Jesus came to this earth, He set forth His life, lifestyle, and the goal of eternal life, leading you to accompany Him in His life, His lifestyle, and His eternal life. You must not forget that you are standing in the historical process of confronting the providential will. 

Jesus established this purpose as the goal of His life over 30 years, leading your ancestors through 2000 years of history to fulfill it. You must feel that there remains a providential responsibility for Jesus to lead your descendants in the future. 

Standing in this position, when Jesus faced the providential will, He could not live a life of ease, nor could He enjoy glory, nor could He meet a day of comfort. 

So, in this time when humanity living on earth cannot find the day of hope that heaven desires, what position should they be in? No matter how much you seek ease, you cannot find it. No matter how much you seek peace in your heart or dream of an ideal and ideological world, you are in a fate where you cannot guarantee it. 

This is because the providence of God, who created heaven and earth, remains a providence of sorrow, and Jesus Christ, who came to fulfill the providence of salvation for fallen humanity, also bears a heart of sorrow while confronting the providential will. Therefore, no one on earth can find ease in their hearts, nor can they boast that they possess the glory of victory. 

As long as God's sorrowful heart remains in the providential fate that must lead humanity, and as long as the sorrowful heart of Jesus Christ, who leads you, remains, and as long as the sorrow of countless saints confronting the providence remains, humanity will never be able to attain the garden of goodness they hope for or the love of God they admire. 

It is not easy for heaven to hold onto humanity in this providence, and what exists there is the condition that Satan blocks and accuses before the sorrowful Father. You must understand this. 

In your life and journey, or in the ideals you desire, if there are elements that do not conform to the heavenly principles or God's creation ideals, you must realize that you are receiving relentless accusations from Satan without exception, and that the Father, the Lord, and the saints are fighting on your behalf, grieving and suffering instead of you. 

Thus, in God's providential history, there is the sorrow of God, the sorrow of Jesus Christ, and the sorrow of countless saints who have confronted the providence until now. But what greater sorrow of God is there? It is the sorrow of having to confront Satan again while defending us. You must understand that this is the position of God. 

Jesus Christ, who sought to narrow the distance between God and humanity, must be contemplated in light of His birth and life. Before Jesus was born on this earth, there was a great distance between humanity and God. Therefore, God wanted humanity to trample all the conditions of the satanic world, that is, to break through the dark powers of Satan who holds the air, and to come up to Him through their utmost efforts. This was the providence of the Old Testament era. 

However, God, knowing that humanity could not possibly come to Him through their own efforts and toil, sent Jesus to this earth. He allowed fallen humanity, who had to look up to heaven with sorrowful tears, to face a central figure who could represent God from a flat perspective. This was the condition for a great victory over Satan in the 4000 years of providential history. 

Yet, because humanity did not believe, the purpose of Jesus' coming to this earth was not fully realized, and thus we are still in a fate where we must pray towards heaven and give our utmost. 

Originally, humanity was created to see and move in a flat perspective, so why has the heart been placed in a position that must look towards heaven? You must fulfill God's providential will within the flat realm for God to be pleased, for Jesus and the Holy Spirit to be pleased, and for all people on earth to be pleased. 

Only when such a time is fulfilled can our hopes be realized. Jesus Christ was sent as the first step to achieve this goal, but due to humanity's disbelief, He had to return. You must understand that you have the responsibility to welcome back the crucified Jesus Christ. 

When Jesus came to this earth, He took the first step in His providential life according to the will of heaven. What was the center of this life? It was to lead people towards God while simultaneously confronting Satan, who accuses humanity. 

Thus, Jesus began from this dual position. In the invisible spiritual realm, He faced accusations from Satan, and in the visible physical realm, He faced opposition from all forms of disbelief. For 4000 years, He bore the sorrow of God's providence, and He wept for the sorrow of the heavenly order. 

With this heart, His gaze was directed towards the people of Israel, and He faced the Judaism chosen according to God's heart of love. However, the nation of Israel, which should have cooperated to fulfill Jesus' mission, and the Judaism that should have accepted God's will, did not appear before Jesus and were all in opposition. 

Today, those who believe this is an inevitable fact must realize that it is time to understand the true heart of Jesus. Jesus had to block the invading forces of Satan spiritually and had to stop all the arrows of disbelief coming from many people physically. 

However, Jesus could not engage in such a battle alone. He was in a position where He had to look towards the greater and further will of God and align His body and heart with it. You must have the heart to sympathize with the life of Christ from the same position. 

For Jesus Christ, who started from this position, the question was how to fulfill God's will, how to subdue Satan, and how to restore fallen humanity. Jesus stepped forward to resolve this. 

The purpose of teaching the way of obedience was that Satan, who held power on earth, had enjoyed God's glory and had governed the humans who should have been under God's dominion. Thus, humanity had lived under the oppression of Satan. 

Therefore, when Jesus came to this earth, He first had to confront the spiritual Satan that caused people to oppose Him, rather than just the people who opposed Him. You must understand that the history of Christianity began from this battle. 

Then, what did Jesus, who appeared to confront the essence of Satan, first manifest within His realm of life? He had to do what Satan could not do. To fulfill this responsibility, He presented practical actions within His realm of life, which is the gospel of Christianity today. 

Both His words and His heart, His life and His lifestyle, and even His death were all aimed at establishing conditions that Satan could not fulfill. You must understand the life journey of Jesus Christ. 

Because there is a heavenly law, in other words, because God governs everything centered on the law, Jesus was able to separate Satan through this heavenly law. 

The essence of Satan is pride and wrath. While Satan, with this nature, dealt with the people of the world, Jesus appeared before them with gentleness and humility. 

Jesus did not stand in a position of humility because He was inferior. He could have been the highest and enjoyed glory more than anyone else, but He gave all that up and stood in a position of gentleness and humility.
188   The providential life of Jesus and his victorious purpose tried to confront Satan, but Jesus knew that there are conditions under which Satan must submit before God, which is why He was able to remain gentle and humble until the end. Thus, Satan appeared with the essence of pride and anger, in contrast to the gentleness and humility that Jesus embodied. Moreover, because Satan is aware of the laws of heaven, he ultimately came to acknowledge Jesus Christ. In other words, when one embodies gentleness and humility, even the world of Satan naturally submits. Knowing this principle, Jesus adopted a position of gentleness and humility that Satan could not emulate. You must understand that by standing in such a gentle and humble position, one can pave a new path to God, who works through the center. Furthermore, what Jesus showed us was obedience and submission. Obedience is following commands in a responsive environment, while submission is following in an unresponsive environment. Jesus taught this principle of obedience and submission to unbelieving humans. This was also to obstruct the essence of Satan and all his living elements. Satan is a being who is centered on himself and does not care about others. This is another aspect of Satan's nature. Therefore, following Satan leads to unhappiness. Jesus taught all humans to believe in Him and to obey Him so that they might follow heaven. However, not understanding this intention of Jesus, people regarded Him as an unjust person before God's will. In such a position, despite receiving indescribable contempt and disdain, Jesus forged ahead on the path of obedience. Additionally, Jesus came forth with the spirit of sacrifice and service. In fact, Jesus, who came to this earth as God's only begotten Son in place of heavenly glory, was in a position to govern all people, all things, and even Satan, and to receive their sacrifices and services, but He stood in the opposite position. In order to make Satan obey, serve, and sacrifice before Him, that is, to subdue all the forces of Satan, Jesus walked the path of infinite sacrifice and service. This is something you must understand.

189 The world of Satan seeks to infinitely utilize and exploit people and creatures, whereas Jesus took the opposite stance. Because Jesus lived a life that Satan could not emulate—being gentle, humble, obedient, submissive, and living a life of sacrifice and service—Satan had to submit in that respect. In other words, Satan cannot obey and submit to God as Jesus did, cannot practice the will with gentleness and humility, and cannot sacrifice and serve on behalf of all humanity before the providential will.

190   The providential life of Jesus and his victorious purpose. Therefore, you must understand that Jesus is the King of kings in goodness, the King of kings in gentleness and humility, the King of kings in obedience and submission, and the King of kings in sacrifice and service. Jesus, throughout 4,000 years of history, saw many people come and go, and many saints appeared, but because He established the highest standards of gentleness, the highest standards of obedience, and the highest standards of sacrifice before heaven, He was able to trample upon all that belonged to the world of Satan. Jesus showed us the bloody path of subduing Satan in this way. Jesus came to this earth and lived a life of gentleness, humility, obedience, submission, sacrifice, and service, and because He possessed the same heart that God had while laboring through a long history concerning this earth, Satan had to fundamentally submit and a historical starting point for fundamental change was established. You must understand this. Satan, knowing God's heart, obstructs the path that humans wish to take toward God and instead leads them to himself. He seeks to elevate himself, to oppose, and to use humans. However, when one approaches God and Jesus, Satan cannot dare to lift his head. You must understand that this condition was established within the realm of Jesus' life. Therefore, when we follow Jesus, Satan is separated from us. The life of Jesus was a life that established such a historical beginning. How did Jesus establish this standard? Jesus first established the standard that God and I are not two but one. If God has eternal life, then I also have eternal life; if God is unchanging, then I am also unchanging; if God is infinitely merciful, then I will also be infinitely merciful. In other words, because Jesus felt God's inner heart better than anyone and could become one with it, He was able to establish the standard of victory in the battle against Satan.

However, since Jesus came and went, until today, no one in the world of Satan has understood the connection of the inner heart between God and Jesus, nor the intricate details and deep-seated issues between God and Satan. 

Gentleness and humility, obedience and submission, sacrifice and service. 2,000 years ago, when Jesus came to this earth and taught humanity to be gentle and humble, to obey and submit, and to sacrifice and serve as a way to subdue Satan, the humans on earth have not had the living environment to be able to be grateful while being gentle and humble, obedient and submissive, and sacrificially serving. As a result, their hearts of obedience unknowingly change into anger and pride, confrontation and rebuttal, and their service and sacrifice turn into exploitation and utilization. 

The reason Jesus was able to resolve these issues was that He had an unbreakable bond with God, and He understood the intricate details that had to be severed between God and Satan, as well as how to separate Satan. However, because humans do not know this, they cannot walk the same path as Jesus. Therefore, you must cry out to heaven, calling out "Father," and pray to Jesus. You must understand God's heart and Jesus' heart and even recognize the schemes of Satan to expose the historical crimes of Satan, to subdue the forces of Satan in reality, and to reveal the secrets of God's providence to settle accounts. 

If you are not gentle and humble, you cannot experience the heart of Jesus. Furthermore, if you do not live a life of obedience and submission, sacrifice and service, you cannot draw near to Jesus. Therefore, to have a correct faith, you must be able to discuss your fundamentals and everything about yourself to unite with the Abel-like existence. However, because Eve did not consult Adam or God after hearing those words of temptation, she made the mistake of falling. God established the law of heaven, saying, “Do not eat,” but the archangel, who denied this, tempted Eve, saying, “For God knows that in the day you eat of it your eyes will be opened, and you will be like God, knowing good and evil” (Genesis 3:5). Such cunning movements of Satan are still occurring today without your knowledge. Therefore, you must be able to discern all the facts happening around you today. Just as a farmer must be able to distinguish between wheat and tares during the harvest season, you must also be able to discern the actions of God and Satan and the results of those actions.

Now, what kind of person must you become? You must become someone who can taste the joy of the harvest. You must be someone who can stand before the Father with dignity. You must bear the fruit of true wheat, not the fruit of tares. Therefore, today you must be able to properly receive the heavenly grace that allows you to grow as true wheat. You must also recognize the time when heaven gives grace. You must understand when the time of new providence for saving fallen humanity is. You must be able to discern everything correctly so that you do not become like tares at the time of God’s new providence and can bear fruit as true wheat. However, humanity has not yet been able to correctly distinguish between truth and falsehood throughout the 6000 years of history. No one has yet borne fruit as true wheat representing human history. Throughout history, countless humans have consistently hoped for the fruit, but no one has borne it. The only one who came to reap it is Jesus Christ, and you must understand this today. Now, you must approach the path of life with a heart that worries and longs for what kind of fruit humanity must bear. Thus, you must become someone who can step into the path of life and give birth to a new second life. Your heart does not always contain only truth. In the field of your heart, both true wheat and tares can be sown. It is not merely that tares are sown in the environment you are in; the elements of fallenness remain in the foundation of your heart. You must understand that the one who walked the path of sacrifice to remove that and purify your heart is none other than Jesus Christ. So, what is your life like? In your daily life...

In this way, you must feel that every single fact arising centered on yourself is at a crossroads of distinguishing between truth and falsehood. Today, within your hearts, there are Cain-like aspects and Abel-like aspects. There are also tares and true grains in your hearts. Therefore, after you take any action, you will always reflect on whether it was Cain-like or Abel-like. The standard for distinguishing between truth and falsehood is that everything exists with the positions of Cain and Abel or the four directions of horizontal and vertical. For this reason, today, wherever you go, you should be able to discern and establish Abel's things as Abel's and Cain's things as Cain's. Even lower animals can discern whether the grass they eat is poisonous or not, so the crown of creation, humanity, must be able to correctly discern all the facts that confront them. You must clearly distinguish who is Cain and who is Abel. If Eve had properly discerned the seductive touch that came upon her in the past, she would not have fallen. If she had fought against Satan with her life relying on God's word until the end, she would not have fallen. However, because she could not discern the illicit desire for something at an inappropriate time, she fell, and you must clearly understand this. Now, before you, there will be tares and true grains. There will also be true shepherds and false shepherds. Therefore, you must now discern them correctly. A true shepherd does not claim to be a true shepherd. At any time, they quietly carry God's will and all creation in their hearts and do not justify their own position. For this reason, when Jesus stood before Pilate's court, the villains claimed they were right, but Jesus did not defend himself. You must reflect on this. However, there may be times at the end when it is difficult to discern what is true and what is false. Therefore, God instructed humans facing such times to anoint their heads with oil and enter the secret place to pray. When everyone claims they are right, extreme confusion and chaos arise, making it impossible to distinguish who is the true shepherd and who is the false shepherd. Thus, you are taught to quietly enter the secret place and pray for judgment. A true son does not boast unless the father boasts of him, nor does he justify himself. Even if he stands in the glory of the father, he does not boast about it but rather seeks to humble himself. Therefore, today, you must continually strive to become such a person. When viewing our church today, you must realize that, although you may not know it, the teacher is engaging in a fierce battle, either spiritually or materially, to pave such a path. Currently, you possess elements that could easily lead you into the dark realm of death. There are many elements centered on your own self, that is, elements that seek to satisfy personal desires, rather than for the whole. For this reason, today, you must deny your insufficient self and entrust everything to the Father, holding the inner heart that says, "Please govern us according to Your will." If you do not possess such a heart and go out, you will inevitably take futile steps, and there will be no way to escape the realm of death ruled by Satan. Now, there will be many tests from Satan on the path you are taking. Additionally, those who communicate with the spiritual world will face many tests. When Satan sees humans fall under his tests, he will accuse them, saying, "Can you succeed like this?" and block your path. Therefore, today, you must have a way to avoid such accusations from Satan, and you know that way well through the principles. Then, what kind of shepherd is a true shepherd? How should true sheep follow the true shepherd? What kind of seed is sown through the true word that bears true grains? What kind of life must you lead to stand in the position of true Abel? You must resolve and overcome these various issues. Thus, you must equip yourselves with the qualifications of Abel so that you can confidently stand before heaven and earth or humanity and all things, and finally avoid the side paths and head toward the true path. You must keep this in mind. The fruits that can enter the true shepherd's storehouse. You should not move recklessly just because something faintly teaches you. You must never move without a clear direction based on absolute truth. If you gossip and confuse it among yourselves, you must clearly understand that a phenomenon similar to the spiritual fall of the angelic world will occur. Now, in this end time, you must have a gift that can be offered to the Father from the position of Abel. If someone else finds out about it, even if that gift is a true grain, it will become a tare. Therefore, today, you must prepare a gift of true grain that no one else can know and sincerely offer it before the Father. Only then can you stand as the true filial son of the Father or as Abel among all the people of this earth, and you will be able to conceive a new life again. And in this end time, you should not just follow the Father's will but also become a leader who guides all people. When the kingdom of the Father is established, you should be able to rejoice as a leader guiding all people and as a true shepherd. To do this, you must become a flock that offers your hidden sincere gift to the Father without relying on anyone's strength. What kind of person is a thief and a robber? They are people who use what does not belong to them as if it were theirs. It seems that there are many such people today. They are using our principles as if they were their own. A correct human is one who returns what they received from heaven with heaven and uses what they received as their own as their own. You must not become a thief or robber who uses heavenly things as their own. Therefore, now you must have certain conditions to stand as an Abel-like being. You must bear true fruits that can enter the true shepherd's storehouse. You must become true fruits and true grains that the true shepherd can rejoice in and enjoy. Flowers that bloom in the spring bear fruit in the autumn, regardless of what kind of flower they are. However, for those flowers to bear abundant fruit in the autumn, they need appropriate temperature, humidity, and nutrients during the growth process. In the same way, for you to bear fruit as an Abel-like being who can receive the heavenly will, you must be able to devote your whole heart to loyalty to heaven, not just today or tomorrow, but for 10, 20, 30, 60 years, and even until the moment of death. Even if you enter the place of death, you must fulfill your duty of faith toward the Father without changing. If you do not become such a person, you will ultimately remain within the realm of Satan and will not be able to stand before the Father as a true Abel. 13) The power of God appears where one heart and one mind are achieved. Amen. <Message> Today, I would like to speak to you under the title "The Power of God Appears Where One Heart and One Mind Are Achieved." The Sadness of the Disciples Who Lost Their Leader. After Jesus resurrected, He stayed on this earth for 40 days, promised to send the Holy Spirit, and ascended. The disciples who followed Jesus rejoiced, believing that the glory of the resurrected Lord meant the fulfillment of God's promise, but Jesus did not give them a definite word about when He would "come again" before He ascended. What must have been the hearts of the disciples at that time? There must have been an indescribable animosity boiling against the unbelieving Israelites and the Jewish authorities who crucified their beloved Lord. If it was the will of the resurrected Lord and the will of God, they must have had the determination to follow the resurrected Lord, even if their bodies turned to dust and their bones melted away, for the final victory. With such determination, that is, with the heart that longed for heaven after the Lord's departure, even if they had to die or if the difficult path of the cross lay before them, they would have encouraged each other whenever they met, saying that they must break through this path.
218   The power of God is revealed where there is one heart and one mind. In this spirit, Jesus appeared to the disciples who were deeply moved and promised to send the Holy Spirit. After that, the 120 disciples gathered in the upper room of Mark experienced a historical providence that they could never have imagined, and they were able to embrace the meaning of all historical providence. They also entered a stage where they could feel the inner heart that Jesus had during His 30 years of private life and 3 years of public ministry. Thus, they could not help but be overwhelmed by the guilt of having betrayed Jesus, realizing that the Jesus who came to this earth was the only begotten Son of Heaven, whom they should not have treated that way. Furthermore, the more they realized that Jesus came to this earth as the Savior of all mankind, the more resolute and determined they became in their hearts, encouraging one another as brothers, apostles, and believers, moving together with one purpose and one heart toward one goal. They exchanged their hearts for the one purpose they pursued and became one, so that although the 120 disciples were each individuals, their direction and actions concerning the Father’s will appeared as one. Such a phenomenon occurred among the apostles, and their hearts burned with passion. What did they then cry out toward? They began to cry out to the Israelite people who opposed Jesus. Moreover, they demonstrated with a new determination and resolve that no one could break the unity of heart they had formed. In this way, they appeared before Heaven with a firm commitment and determination, and regardless of how severe the persecution was, when they manifested a steadfast center, Heaven established each of them as representatives of Jesus and entrusted them with their mission. You must understand that there was not just one person with such a heart. The greater the sorrow of losing the Lord, the more deeply they felt it, and the stronger the movement of God’s will became, the stronger their animosity toward the group that betrayed Heaven surged. When they resolved to crush them in a day and an hour and to fulfill Heaven’s will immediately, the power of God, which is not human, was manifested. We must recognize that here was demonstrated the direct exercise of God’s authority, which is unimaginable to humans, shown to the ignorant, unbelieving, and rebellious people. The 120 disciples, who united to reveal God’s power, would not have made Christianity a global religion today if they had not gathered in the upper room of Mark, believing in the promise of the Holy Spirit and praying as one. At that time, the 120 disciples who prayed prostrate had no fear. They forgot their prestige, their face, and their families, and solely believed that the Lord's promise would be manifested at some time and place. When the 120 disciples became one and prayed, the Holy Spirit descended upon the earth, breaking through the authority of death that had been blocking the way between Heaven and earth for 4,000 years. This was not a coincidence. Because of this event, a new path was opened that could give birth to humanity again. Who accomplished this? It was achieved by the earnest hearts of the 120 disciples who looked to the Father’s will, God, with one heart, one spirit, and one sacrificial mindset. You must understand that the work of the Holy Spirit, which could not govern the earth, was finally able to make a new historical start. When the 120 disciples experienced the work of the Holy Spirit, where Heaven and earth trembled and tongues of fire were divided, their earnest hearts toward Heaven were deeply moved, and they gained the mindset to face any enemies, prepared to confront death. Here, the power of Heaven was again applied, a power that no one could sever. Because this power served as a stepping stone, you must understand that what they said exercised the ability to move Heaven and earth. 
220   The power of God is revealed where there is one heart and one mind. So how can we fulfill God’s will today? First, we must possess a heart that can become one with God. If there are ten thousand people on this earth, each of those ten thousand people has different intentions. However, since God’s will is one, we must trample our own intentions and remove all conditions we present, following the Father’s will and conditions. Even if our intentions and hearts are different and our positions and environments vary, if we do not become one with the Father’s will, God’s will cannot be fulfilled. They centered on God’s will, feeling as though “I am you, and you are me,” merging into one heart and one spirit. Therefore, when someone faced a difficult situation, they did not leave it as an individual’s problem but regarded it as their own difficulty. To become one in heart and mind, you must become someone who can forget everything, including material possessions, social honors, social status, power, and influence. If this is blocked, you must become someone who can bravely overcome it, just as the apostles performed miraculous signs by defeating ignorant enemies through the work of the Holy Spirit in the upper room. You must have such a heart and pray, "Let us become one in heart, let us become one in mind, let one action be manifested." This is the slogan we must shout at this time. If there is someone who blocks this and prevents it from being realized, they are indeed an enemy of heaven. Do you wish for a great purpose to be fulfilled today? Then you must become one in heart. Do you wish for great glory to be revealed? Every individual must become one. Where hearts become one, everything connects. It can endure infinitely. Therefore, we must quickly become one in heart today. Is there an element in your heart that cannot become one? You must recognize this as the enemy and understand that this is the great Satan. This is what leads you to hell. Satan is taking you away. This condition will cause you to stand at the judgment seat. You must remove such conditions from your life and organize them from your environment with the determination to unify your hearts and minds, becoming one as the substitute for the Father’s heart and the Father’s will, until we can subdue Satan. This is not just about today. Even if there are remnants of Satan for ten years, you must be able to unite with one person for ten years and unite with a thousand people for ten years until the Father’s will is fulfilled. We must dedicate our lives to fighting against Satan and ultimately subdue Satan so that we can reveal the Father’s glory while we are alive. You must keep this in mind.

<Prayer> If the heart of the Father and the heart of Adam had become one, and if the will of the Father and the will of Adam had become one, there would not have been the sorrowful history of two worlds fighting against each other today. Today, in our hearts, there is the sorrowful heart and the sad heart of the Father. The true heart acknowledges this, but the fallen nature centered on oneself denies it. I know that I am always in this battle between the true heart and the selfish heart, so today, please allow us to tidy up our own hearts and unite with the Father’s heart. The time is approaching when we must tidy up our own will to unite with God’s will, so if there is any heart among these sons and daughters that cannot unite with the Father, please forgive us. Please allow us to forget everything about ourselves and strive only to unite with the Father’s heart and the Father’s will. We know that the heart united with the Father’s heart is a heart that cannot be exchanged for thousands of millions, so please lead us to be able to fight and protect that one heart, even if it means sacrificing everything. Loving Father, we earnestly hope and wish for this. Father, this time is extremely difficult, and Satan is blocking our hearts from becoming one, so we earnestly hope and wish for you to allow us to establish a new organization that sacrifices oneself for others to fulfill the Father’s will. We earnestly hope and wish for you to allow us to carry out the providential work that can fight for the Father’s will and expand the glory of the Father’s will. May the hearts and minds of us gathered today be established as one before the Father’s altar, serving as a condition of the Father’s connection that wishes to subdue Satan, and we earnestly hope for this, and we pray all these things in the name of the Lord. Amen.

*14) Let us celebrate Christmas in place of heaven. Luke 2:1 - It can be seen that God's providence, which has been carried out for 4000 years since Adam, was fulfilled through the birth of Jesus. You must think once again that the time when God's will is fulfilled and human will is fulfilled was that one hour when Christ was born. Although 2000 years have passed since the birth of Jesus Christ, we feel that we are now in a historical and cosmic tense time where God's will is being fulfilled and human will is being fulfilled, just like when Jesus was born 2000 years ago. The meaning of the birth of Jesus Christ - Although Jesus was born as a small bundle of flesh, He is the reality that can represent God's will. His cries and movements can substitute for God's 4000 years of grievances and typify all that God wishes to newly work on this earth, as well as express the sorrows of the 4000-year historical process of atoning for human sin. Therefore, with His birth, we were able to meet the joyful scene where a new history of goodness begins.

15) The Significance of the Trinity Expectation 
You have organized the Trinity Expectation, but you may not fully understand its heavenly value. You know the meaning of restoration through the Principle. So, what will you restore? What did Jesus have to restore on this earth? What was Jesus' central responsibility in the providence of restoration? It was to find the number that was lost in the Adam family. Jesus came to this earth with the mission to restore this. 

The significance of the number in the providence of restoration 
Therefore, in the Adam family, there were eight members centered around Adam, including Adam himself, his three sons, and their partners. God worked for 1600 years to restore these eight members. He chose Noah to uphold the providential will for 120 years and established Noah's eight members. 

From Adam, God established Noah through ten generations, and due to Ham's mistake, the will could not be upheld any longer, so it was extended for another ten generations down to Abraham. However, because Abraham made a mistake in offering sacrifices, it was extended for two more generations. Thus, it was only during Jacob's time that a stage of the 2000-year providence was concluded. You should know this.

Only then can I attain eternal life.So, when you wake up in the morning, ask yourself, “For whom will I revolve today? Genesis 3:1-14

Through this scripture, we can understand the motivation for the beginning of humanity's sorrow, as well as the fact that our human ancestors were expelled from God's embrace. God created all things through the ideal of creation and then made Adam and Eve as central beings of the universe who could enjoy being with God and all creation. However, due to their fall, God's purpose of creation remained unfulfilled, and God came to regret having created humanity. This was God's sorrow and the groaning of all creation. The happiness and hope of humanity, which should have been centered on the eternal ideal of goodness, came to a halt from this point. When we reflect on the fundamental destruction of hope for God and humanity, the Creator and all creation, we must realize that there lies the sorrow of humanity and the sorrow of God.

When God created all things, He poured out all His sincerity and effort. Moreover, on January 5, 1958, at the former headquarters church, this message was summarized in the 28th issue of the "Sermon Summary" by the Young Adult Evangelical Department. 

When God created Adam and Eve, the protagonists of all creation, He devoted all His energy and effort, creating them as a temple where He could dwell. You know well through the Principle that God created all things so that they could live with humanity forever, enjoying their presence, and that humanity could rejoice while God rejoiced. Although God established this purpose of creation, He has never been able to experience such a time due to Adam's fall. Therefore, you must keep in mind that God seeks to find such a time again.

You must understand the sorrowful heart of God when He called out to Adam after the fall, saying, "Adam, Adam!" Although God was in a position to reject Adam and Eve, who had rejected the Creator, He called out to Adam again, "Adam, Adam!" This calling was not just for Adam and Eve but was a historical calling. We must recognize that the inner heart of God, who called Adam after creation, has been unknown to humanity until today. The voice that called out to Adam at that time has become a message of sorrow that has replaced 6,000 years of history. We must understand that God called Adam with a sorrowful heart that represented the entire grief of creation that has been under the dominion of the fall since the beginning. Although 6,000 years have passed since Adam, we must recognize that God is still calling us, the second Adam and Eve, in the present day, connecting the events of that time to the current age.

Faithful believers who have emerged after the fall have felt this heart of God, lamenting for the land where humanity cannot hear God's voice calling Adam and Eve, and they have mourned in place of God. We must understand the heartbreaking heart of God who called Adam and Eve after the fall, realizing the sorrow of a Father who faced the fallen state of Adam, who had entered a place not permitted. 

Heaven is calling us, and when we embrace that heart and share the same sorrow, God can once again carry out His providence of salvation for humanity on this earth. You must not forget that God has been calling you through countless prophets and sages throughout history. The voice that called out to the fallen Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden is still echoing today. God has called Adam with a sincere heart for 1,600 years after the fall, and only when He could hold onto Noah, who could be faithful to heaven, could He finally call out, "Noah, Noah!" We must learn to hear that historical voice.

To fulfill the heart of God who called Adam, He called Noah. However, who among the people understood the Father's heart, which was worried for 120 years after calling Noah? No one on earth understood that God had called Noah for the sake of a day of restoration, worrying for 120 years. If there is someone among you who can feel God's sorrow over losing Adam and Eve, God cannot treat that person without tears. If there is someone who can feel the sorrowful heart of God when Adam, who should have remained in a blessed position, was expelled from God's embrace, that person cannot help but repent before God on behalf of Adam.

The sorrow of heaven began with the fall of Adam. Because of this, God, who has been filled with grief, is now appealing to you with a heart full of sorrow. If we understand this fact, we will weep and mourn to the depths of our bones and flesh, and our hearts will be filled with sorrow without end. Among the prophets and sages who have come and gone throughout history, there has not been a single person who did not shed tears of sorrow. Those who stood for God did not avoid the path of suffering. Noah did, Abraham did, and Isaac and Jacob did as well. Not only individuals but also Moses, who represented a nation, and Jesus, who represented the world as the Savior of all, also did.

Today, we must mourn as God mourns, and we must share in God's sorrow when He grieves. The fact that Adam and Eve forgot God and sought joy centered on themselves has left a condition of sorrow in the historical journey. This sorrowful land was created because Adam and Eve betrayed God's will and acted selfishly, forgetting the heavenly principles. And where did God's sorrow originate? It began when humanity forgot the sorrow of heaven and the grief of God, seeking only their own satisfaction and comfort. Therefore, we must become the crystallization of the tears of the prophets and sages who have come and gone throughout history.

We must become representatives of heaven in distress and anguish, understanding the sorrow, anger, and injustice of heaven and fighting against evil. In doing so, we must fulfill our mission to comfort heaven by defending the Father, Jesus, and the historical prophets and sages. The Father is seeking such people. You must understand that Jesus, the Holy Spirit, and all our ancestors who have come to this earth have sought such beings.

How many hours have you spent in the position of being rejected and mocked by all people on behalf of heaven, while living a life that has been cleared of the past? Fallen humanity is in a historical journey of sad fate, so those who seek heaven cannot avoid this path. This has become the ironclad rule of the fallen world. For this reason, God has been the God of those who mourn throughout the historical process. He is the God who has grieved as He has seen His sons and daughters being trampled by evil forces while unfolding the providence of His will. However, God does not wish to remain in sorrow forever. He desires to quickly escape from sorrow, anguish, and resentment and to welcome the day of joy.

Although 6,000 years of history have passed since the fall of humanity, there has not been a single son or daughter who could celebrate the glory of heaven on the day of joy until now. Therefore, the Christianity established by heaven is a religion of tears. Christianity is a religion of the cross. The path walked by Jesus and the path walked by the Jewish people were marked by valleys of tears and the way of the cross. The wider this gap, the greater God's sorrow and resentment became.

To turn this opposing path back into a relative path, the history of struggle has unfolded over the 2,000 years since Jesus. You must understand that this is the historical journey of faith. Now, place yourself among all creation and critically examine yourself, separating your heart and body. Stand before God and be judged. The more you think about it, the more you cannot deny that you are deserving of the consequences of sin.

Our many ancestors have passed through the altar of historical blood and tears. Today, God wishes to place you on that altar and establish you as a victorious fruit. If you do not know this and reject that will, where will that nation go? Where did the people who opposed the chosen Abraham go? If we want to leave something to boast about in history, we must become those who can say, "Oh, Father! Please pass that sorrow onto me," to replace God's sorrow. A nation that prays, "I will carry the burden that You bear," will not perish. How many people in this world can follow such a person?

Therefore, we must shed tears on behalf of God's sorrow, we must weep for humanity whom the Father loves, we must weep for Noah's sorrow, and we must become those who can weep for the 6,000 years of sorrow from Adam to Abraham, Isaac, Jacob, Moses, Jesus, and up to today. If there is someone who can respond to God's voice, calling out for a son or daughter on this earth, saying, "Father, here I am," even if that person is unkempt, wounded in heart, and shabby in appearance, they will not perish. The path of such a person cannot be blocked even if the world is mobilized; this is the principle of heavenly law. Because Jesus knew this principle, He mourned for the betraying Israel, shed tears for the persecuting sect, and could bless even those who nailed Him to the cross.

Today, those who believe must stand before heaven and also stand as brides before the Bridegroom, Jesus. What is heaven trying to announce to the world through you today? The time for shedding tears for oneself has already passed. Now is the time for world unity, so the time for shedding tears for families has also passed. God's sorrow has passed through individuals, families, societies, and nations. Now, He mourns for the world.

God's intention regarding Adam and Eve
So, on what basis did God create this created world? He began to create all things through the eternal and unique Word. Thus, God's purpose in creating Adam and Eve was that they would fulfill the purpose of that Word and become a body in which God could dwell eternally. Furthermore, God breathed life into Adam and Eve, intending to dwell in their hearts as the subject of eternal life and establish a resting place. This was the great purpose of heaven's providence in creating Adam and Eve. In other words, God created Adam and Eve and sought to establish the laws of heavenly life through the Word, and He desired to create a temple where God could personally dwell through their bodies, and He wished to establish a holy of holies in their hearts where God could directly sit. However, due to Adam's fall, the laws of providence that could replace the Word disappeared before humanity. When Adam, who was created as God's body, fell, the temple where God could dwell also vanished from the human world. Moreover, the foundation of the heart where the incorporeal God could dwell as the protagonist of this earthly reality also disappeared. In this way, because humanity fell, the laws that replaced the Word, which is the ideology of creation, the body that could replace the temple of all things, and the heart that could replace the holy of holies of the incorporeal world all deviated from their original purpose, and from here, God's sorrow began. Consequently, the heart of humanity, created for heaven, became sorrowful, and the body that was to respond to that heart also became sorrowful, and the laws that could replace the Word, which would allow that heart and body to move, disappeared from humanity. 
When we examine these fundamental principles and contents of heaven, we must ask where the laws of the Word that heaven is seeking will manifest among the countless people born on this earth with the bloodline of sin due to the fall. Where will the substantial temple where God can dwell appear? Where will the holy of holies that can replace the incorporeal world appear on this earth? Many people throughout history have tried to solve these questions. You must understand that many of our prophets and ancestors have gone through a process of shedding blood and tears, sacrificing many lives to achieve this purpose. Therefore, now a being possessing a Word that can be called the first in heaven and the first on earth must appear on this earth. A being equipped with the substantial temple of the invisible God, a being that can be rejoiced in and defended by God, a being of universal value representing heaven and earth must emerge. For this reason, you must clearly understand today that a foundation of power that can replace the heavenly world and the Father's throne, as well as embody the substantial ideology that can move the created world, is God's hope, humanity's hope, and the hope of all believers who must be saved today. 
261 So, what have we humans lost? This is the Word of God, which is greater than any individual's thought or any Word on this earth, and is the hope of all humanity. When we look at today's reality, there is a religion that replaces the realm of metaphysical truth and a natural science that replaces the realm of physical truth. Where will these lead? Because Adam and Eve lost the Word due to the fall, they lost the substance, and by losing the substance, they lost the ideology. This must be restored through a central figure at the end. Therefore, a being standing at the forefront of scientific civilization must appear as a substantial being that replaces all metaphysical ideologies in this end times of human history. 
So, when we look at ourselves today, where should we humans be heading? However, while our hearts wish to do good and strive for heaven, our bodies are entangled in the two opposing paths of doing evil and turning toward the world. This is the state of humanity today. Thus, humanity has been constantly searching for the owner who possesses the heavenly Word that can unify these two and where the laws of heavenly truth are.
