On the other hand, if you have experienced and felt something in the spiritual world from the standpoint of being one with the heavenly principles that represent your body and life, and your essence that represents those principles, you will not disappear from this earth forever. Therefore, you must establish a core that cannot disappear forever in your body and heart. 

You must establish an inseparable heavenly principle in your body and heart, creating a resting place where God can personally be present. 

Where is the resting place where heaven can be present? You must reflect on whether you have become someone who can accept such words of the heavenly principles. Now that the end has come, everything will come to an end. Philosophy will end, science will end, and the global economic system centered on material will also come to an end. 

At some point in the future, food developed through scientific research efforts due to the infinite development of science may emerge. Furthermore, today, at the end of the final days, you must repent of your faith until now and strive to live according to the words that Jesus has given us. Therefore, you must seek the words of the Father. 

However, if there are those who try to abandon those words instead of seeking them, they will surely be judged. Those who avoid or obstruct the words that come to establish the heavenly holy place will perish. Because Jesus knew this content, he could not fully express everything he wanted to say. 

Therefore, the more you feel the mission to establish the heavenly principles, the more you must do your best. You must become those who can resolve the sorrowful heart of Jesus, who said, "If you do not believe when I speak of earthly things, how will you believe when I speak of heavenly things?" (John 3:12). 

You must understand that there is historical sorrow at the end of human history that permeates heaven and earth today. Therefore, God is looking down upon all humans, worrying about how they are living on this earth and how the believers are believing. 

Thus, you must have the heart to accept the words that represent the infinite universe and the eternal principles. You cannot proceed with the earthly heart you have lived with until now or with any words that come from earthly emotions. You must have a new heart that can accept new words. 

Therefore, in this end time, you must be careful not to become a successor to Adam, who betrayed the words of the heavenly principles. 

So, where did sin begin? It began from not receiving God's words. It was the responsibility of humans to accept the infinite words of God, but they failed to fulfill that responsibility. Therefore, your heart must become the resting place that welcomes the words. 

Thus, you must establish a reality centered on the words. Those words are connected to your personal realm. In other words, your words must become words that represent God's heavenly principles, and your actions must become actions that are united with those words of principles. 

Just as you know through the principles, when the reality that represents the words appears, God's heart will be present there. Therefore, the being where God's heart is present will move in a direction that can communicate the eternal ideals, allowing that body and heart to live in a way that can represent the ideals of the Father in the actual living realm. 

Desiring to live such a life is our hope, and the place where that purpose is fulfilled is the ideal garden of Canaan, the lost original garden. You must surely understand this. 

The saints who must become the bride of Jesus 

Then, what was the sorrow of Jesus? It was the sorrow of having no resting place for the words. It was also the sorrow of having no saints who could hand over the will of his heart and body. Not only was there no one to hand over his words, but there was also no one to receive his body as the body of God. This was the sorrow of Jesus, the sorrow of God, and the sorrow of all humanity. 

Thus, God and Jesus, throughout the 2,000 years of history, have said, "I am the bridegroom, and you are the bride," entrusting the body of Jesus to you, who are like a bride, hoping to meet a day of rest. You must understand that God and Jesus have been working behind the scenes to establish that day until now. 

So, if you say you live with the words of God, what should you do? First, you must create an environment where you can live immersed in God's words, and you must qualify as a bride who can meet the bridegroom, Jesus. God is still longing for a being who can be the counterpart of Jesus to appear at this time. 

God wants to entrust to you Jesus, who is the heavenly prince, the master of all creation, and the savior of humanity. Furthermore, the earnest heart that Jesus had for all humanity must also arise in your own heart and body. 

Therefore, Jesus has been seeking a bride who can represent his ideals and can replace all his intentions for 2,000 years. 18) Let us cross the historical peak of misfortune.

280 We earnestly ask and wish to overcome the historical peak of misfortune. In the name of the Lord, we pray. Amen. <Message> The title of the message I would like to reflect on with you for a moment is "Let Us Overcome the Historical Peak of Misfortune." I will speak briefly with this title. 

The path of misfortune we must overcome. Even though countless people live in this world today, you know well that there is an unavoidable path of misfortune ahead of them that they cannot avoid. From the perspective of Christian thought, there is judgment at the end. Thus, many Christians have lived with the concern of how to overcome this peak of death. When you reflect on your current state, the more you acknowledge that you are unknowingly placed in a state of sorrowful destiny, the more you will feel that serious problems are hanging before you, around you, or in your heart and body. 

We have the mission to break free from such unfortunate circumstances today, and this is the mission for the remainder of our lives. Only when that day comes, when you can step over the environment of sorrow, can you step over the history of misfortune of the past, and only by stepping over this can you welcome the garden of hope of a new day. 

When we find ourselves in such a situation and reflect on the history of the past, you must realize that the peak of misfortune or the environment you are facing is not faced by you alone. You should understand that our ancestors also went through the path of misfortune over the long span of 6000 years. 

As you trace back through history, you must feel that our ancestors were in a position where they could not escape the misfortune between humanity and the Creator. You must feel this desperate heart in place of history or the ideal of creation centered on yourself, and you must have a day of joy when you can say that you have achieved victory in place of history. Otherwise, happiness, hope, and ideals in today's human society will all be cut off. 

Because humanity has gone through this historical process, God has felt the responsibility of how to break through the veil of misfortune that has been cast over the spirit and life of humanity through history. Those who have come out seeking the way have also come out with a sense of responsibility to solve this one issue for humanity. If it is said that the countless religions that have existed until now have left unresolved tasks, it means that they have left behind the mission to solve this problem. 

You know that heaven is mobilized to break through these barriers of misfortune that remain for humanity. You must understand that heaven is mobilized to overcome this destiny of misfortune, and that the spirit world of the other world is also mobilized. Furthermore, you must know that humans on earth are also mobilized. 

Because humanity has failed to find the historical moment to step over the barriers of misfortune, we have inherited this history of misfortune today. Therefore, we must now unite and step over all these barriers of misfortune. If we cannot step over this, you must understand that your descendants will also have to overcome the barriers of misfortune, and that they cannot avoid the paths of death, sorrow, and tears that our ancestors walked. 

When you think about this, you can realize that you are not a simple existence today. You carry the heavenly longing within you, and the longing of humanity is deeply embedded in you. Furthermore, you stand in a position to resolve the entire longing of the past, present, and future. 

If you cannot pioneer and overcome all these barriers of misfortune with your one day of life or one lifetime, the historical hope or providential hope that has been looking at you, or the heavenly hope that has been trying to overcome the barriers of misfortune through you will be shattered. When you think about this, you must realize that you are not an individual today. 

Today, there are many people, but how many can stand as responsible individuals who can fight against the invisible Satan and the forces of evil that block us, representing the misfortune of God, the misfortune of angels, and the misfortune of future humanity? 

When you think about this, you must understand that we are not the only ones who have faced this position today; countless prophets and sages who have dealt with God's providence until now have also fought to solve this one problem while sacrificing their lives in the same circumstances. You must feel this deeply in your bones. 

The miserable fate of Noah. When you reflect on the Old Testament era, look at Noah. Noah was the one who was found among many people after laboring for 1600 years since God left behind the miserable fate of humanity. What kind of being was this Noah? He was to have the heart to feel the heavenly misfortune on behalf of the countless humanity of that time, and he stood in a position to comfort God on behalf of the misfortune felt by the people of that time. 

Noah, who was in such a position, bearing the historical mission of 1600 years, fought in a position of misfortune that no one had ever felt in history, being trampled, mocked, driven, and persecuted for the sake of humanity and heaven. You must not forget the life of Noah. 

So what appeared before Noah's life? It was the ark that represented the sorrowful circumstances of misfortune that God had hoped for over 1600 years to establish the principle of indemnity. The ark that Noah had to face was a being that represented the historical misfortune. 

Because he felt the mission to overcome the peak of misfortune of 1600 years, God, who entrusted him with this responsibility, and Noah, who bore this responsibility, became one heart. Noah knew that the ark was given as a historical condition of indemnity, which is why he walked the path of harsh misfortune and tribulation for 120 years. 

After being warned that the land would be judged in 120 years, Noah began to build the ark with all his sincerity from that day. However, it was not just one year, but after enduring a long period of 120 years to build the ark, Noah's heart in building the ark was not for his family. It was not with the heart of building for his descendants. It was certainly not with the heart of building for the wicked world of that time. 

Only, the heart in building this ark was to fulfill the will of God. In this way, you must reflect on the figure of Noah, who silently fought while embracing the sorrow of God and the sorrow of countless prophets and sages who had come through over 1600 years. 

When you think about this, we must understand that although our ancestors who upheld God's will in the past walked a sorrowful path, Noah, who was in such an environment, pushed away and overcame the difficult environment the more difficult circumstances came, and he underwent an infinite internal struggle of body and mind. 

He fought for 120 years. In a situation where no one sympathized with him, Noah devoted himself to establishing God's will and maintained his integrity. When you think about this, you can see that Noah's heart was truly one of sorrow that no ancestor had felt after 1600 years. 

After going through such a process, heaven finally recognized him, and when the time came, a day came when God's promise was fulfilled, and there was a judgment that could resolve the grievances of misfortune. The more Noah bore the great mission of providence, the more he could not live an easy life. 

He could not live a joyful and peaceful life. His body suffered pain, his heart suffered anguish, and he was persecuted by the environment of sin. In this way, after overcoming the difficult peak where no one sympathized with him, heaven was able to side with him, and after enduring 120 years of persecution, sorrow, and indescribable misfortune, God finally appeared as a friend and comforter to Noah, taking on the responsibility of resolving Noah's misfortune. 

However, you must understand that Noah had to engage in relentless struggle in both his internal and external life until the promise was fulfilled. Noah himself did not know that there were both internal and external barriers of misfortune. God's providential will was not completed merely by building the external ark. 

After building the ark, there was the execution of God's judgment, and thereafter, he was in a position to build a new family in the restored garden. In this way, Noah did not know that after everything seemed to end with the ark, there remained the internal peak of misfortune. Ultimately, due to the mistakes of that day, Noah's family fell. 

Abraham and Jacob, who had to bear the entire misfortune. Abraham, who inherited Noah's will and was chosen as the ancestor of faith 400 years later, also bore the mission to overcome the barriers of misfortune between heaven and earth alone. Thus, Abraham could not avoid the path that Noah had walked. 

Therefore, after Abraham left behind his beloved hometown, that is, after receiving God's command to leave Ur of the Chaldeans, he began to experience a life of misfortune that he had never encountered before. After leaving Ur of the Chaldeans, or after passing through Egypt and returning to the land of Canaan, until he found Lot and established the condition for the restoration of all things, he had to feel the sorrow that those who sought heaven until then had not felt. 

There were no relatives. There were no companions. There were no friends. Nevertheless, Abraham had to bear the overall feelings of misfortune of humanity from the position of having to take responsibility for the entire history of restoration. Therefore, regardless of what peak of misfortune might come, what hardships might arise, what sorrows might come, or what difficulties and pains might follow, you must understand the life of misfortune of Abraham, who overcame everything with the heart to fulfill God's remaining will. 

Thus, although the effort until he set up the altar and offered the three sacrificial offerings was great, Abraham himself did not know that the internal sorrow centered on the offerings would strike him. Therefore, we must reflect on Abraham's position again. 

While Abraham was in an environment of misfortune, he had to realize that being in this environment was not for himself, but that he had to take on the historical mission, the mission of the times, and even the mission of future descendants and the heavenly mission. However, Abraham had not thought of that yet. 

He thought that by overcoming the external barriers of misfortune that remained, everything would be resolved, but he did not know that he had to resolve not only the misfortune of his time but also the misfortune of the future. Abraham was to establish a point of restoration in the eternal history of humanity, but he failed to do so. 

Thus, although Abraham stepped over the internal life of misfortune and reached the point of offering Isaac, it was not resolved, and the internal misfortune has come down to us today. However, you must understand that Abraham, who was responsible for the historical misfortune, was in a pitiful position. 

So how many times did Abraham resolve to take on the responsibility with the heart of misfortune that no human had felt until then? He swore that at any moment, whether awake or asleep, if he forgot that he was a sacrifice centered on God's will, the will of God would be fulfilled.
286   We were concerned that we could not cross the historic peak of misfortune. We mourned for heaven and thought we must dedicate ourselves for heaven. You must understand the tragic heart of Abraham. When it comes to Jacob, from the day he received the mission to inherit Abraham's foundation and fulfill the blessings of heaven, Jacob lived a life of misfortune. Not only did he live a life of misfortune for 21 long years in the house of Laban in Haran, but he also lived a life of overcoming Esau internally. You must understand that there was always a sad condition on the path Jacob took. 

The reason Moses and the Israelite people could not overcome misfortune was similar. For Moses, who bore the mission to restore the nation for 400 years after Abraham, the 40 years of preparation in the royal palace to face God's will, the 40 years of living in the Midian wilderness where he was in the stage of practicing that will, and the 40 years of leading 600,000 people from Egypt toward Canaan in the wilderness were all unspeakable periods of misfortune. 

Moreover, there were times when he ascended Mount Sinai alone, harboring the tragic feelings unknown to the nation, to negotiate before heaven on behalf of the nation. Leaving 600,000 people in the wilderness, he forgot everything about his 80-year life and the sorrowful circumstances he was facing at that time, heading toward Mount Sinai. You must be able to empathize with Moses' tragic heart as he pleaded and implored before heaven, forgetting all food and drink during the time of sacrifice. No one among the Israelite people understood the solemn heart of Moses as he wrestled and poured out his body and mind before heaven. 

When you consider this, you can see that none of our ancestors who bore the mission of restoration from Noah until now felt the sorrowful life and the path of misfortune they were appealing for, and no one followed them. Thus, the prophets and sages in heaven lament, asking who can take responsibility for the misfortunes and grievances they left behind while fighting on behalf of heaven. If you do not take responsibility for that misfortune, they will accuse you. 

The entire nation had the mission to enter the Canaan welfare permitted by God, yet they complained and wanted to sit down in the wilderness. At such times, the nation did not know that Moses struggled to offer one life as a living sacrifice to save the lives of the entire nation. Only God knew. Only God became his friend, and only God treated him as a father. 

Because Moses knew such a God, he forgot food for 40 days and felt a sense of responsibility that he would not let the Father have sorrow and tragic feelings again. By pleading with all his heart, he received the words that could resurrect the Israelite people. This was a joyful matter. However, to introduce joy, the Israelite people did not know that there was someone who became a sacrificial offering of sorrow behind the scenes. If they had known this, the 600,000 people in the wilderness would not have fallen. Even after that, if they had faith that they would uphold Moses' Ten Commandments and would not bend even if their bodies became sacrifices to resolve heaven's sorrowful heart, they would not have fallen in the wilderness.

The center of hope for humanity and all creation
Today, many people live on this earth. They each have their own visions and opinions, and they live with various claims. However, there is no one who can confidently stand before heaven and earth, worshiping God with their heart and body, claiming to be sent by God. Many people today are living with their own visions and claims, but if their claims and actions do not align with the will of heaven and the providence of heaven, they will inevitably be overturned at some point, as we have seen many times throughout history. 

So what is it that we humans must ultimately seek? It is to abandon all our claims and subjective actions, and to come forth claiming that our hearts and bodies represent God and that we act on behalf of God. Many people who have come and gone throughout history have hoped for this. Heaven also desires such representatives and has been working with infinite effort and patience for a long time. You must understand this well. 

Thus, the sorrow of this earth is not due to the absence of a certain claim, nor is it due to the absence of acting individuals. The sorrow and sadness arise from the lack of a claim that can represent God's heart and will, and from the absence of individuals who can act on behalf of God. Today, to remove all the sighs, pains, and deep-seated grievances that are scattered in this world and among humanity, there must appear a person who can represent God's claims and act on behalf of God. Therefore, you must realize that the purpose of providence is this one person, and the purpose of history is also this one person. 

The creation ideal that God desired was to dwell with all creation centered on humanity, but it was not realized on this earth due to the fall of our ancestors, Adam and Eve. All beings created by God through His word over six days were meant to fulfill that word. In other words, all creation is the substantial object of God's word. Then, after all creation appeared as substantial objects through the word, what did it desire? It desired to become a mediator, a center that could move when God moves and settle when God settles, centered on God's love. If humanity had become such a center, the chaotic history that has unfolded on this earth would not have existed. 

God's hope is for one being who can represent God and act on behalf of God to appear. This is not something that God has desired only after the fall of humanity but has been the center of hope since the time of creation until now. You must understand this. 

The being who came as the substance of the word
Then what kind of being is the center of this hope? He is the being who represents the word and is the substance of the word. At the same time, He must become the substance of life centered on God's love. This is the problem. Only when He becomes the substance of life can He fulfill the substantial form that can represent God's image and can appear with a claim that can represent God's word. You must understand this. 

Among the words of the Bible, there is a saying, “I am the way, the truth, and the life” (John 14:6). In other words, Jesus is the way, the truth, and the life. What does this signify to all humanity? It signifies that because Adam and Eve fell, God's word was not fulfilled, and that word returned to God's heart, but since there are still people living on this earth who have lost the word, God has given this word back to humanity. 

Because of the connection between the words that God spoke at the time of creation and humanity, we have been hoping for that unchanging goal, that one hope, until now. Therefore, to fulfill this word, the substance of the word must come. Where has the substance on this earth that can represent God's word gone? You must understand that the journey of searching for this substance is the path of providence that God has walked for 6000 years. All creation, made in six days, possesses the substance of the word, yet humanity, created on the sixth day, has not been able to stand before God's word with the substance of the word, and has continued down to this day. You must understand that establishing the substance of the word is God's path of destiny, the path of restoration, and the historical path. 

Thus, when Jesus said, “I am the way, the truth (that is, the word), and the life” (John 14:6), this indicates that the substance of God's word that God has hoped for is Jesus. Therefore, what were Jesus' words? They were the words that represented God's earnest heart, which God had wanted to express to humanity over the 4000 years of history. You must understand that the one who came as the protagonist of the word for this purpose is Jesus. 

In this way, Jesus was the one who appeared as the substance of the word that God had sought for 4000 years. The word that was in God's heart needed to be manifested through the created world, but it could not be realized. However, through the appearance of Jesus, the word that was in God's heart could be transferred to Jesus' heart. You must understand that this fact is the most joyful news for humanity. 

So when Jesus appeared as the historical substance of the word and opened His mouth to declare the word, what must He have felt? What kind of heart would He have had? Jesus felt that His words were the words that represented the will of historical providence. He also felt that His words represented the words that were in God's heart, and He felt that these words could repeatedly carry out the work of re-creation on behalf of God until God's will and the substance of the word are fulfilled on this earth. 

Therefore, to receive Jesus' words today, we must understand that Jesus is not merely someone who passed through a simple 30 years of life, and that His words are not merely words to justify the course of life in that era. Jesus' words are words that can represent 4000 years of history, can substitute for the world of that time, and can represent the history of humanity up to now. However, at that time, there was no one who recognized the value of Jesus' words. What was God's lament? It was that all creation, made by the word, did not appear as the substance of the word. The word and the substance

They became enemies before Jesus. The Israelite nation and the Jewish nation were to be established as a foothold for the global restoration, and centered around this foothold, Jesus Christ was to launch a full-scale war for the global return to Canaan. However, due to Jesus' death, He found Himself in a situation similar to that of Moses, and thus, until today, Christianity has been in a wilderness period. You must understand that, like the Israelite nation that lost its master, it remains in the wilderness.

Then, when Jesus came to this earth, He was supposed to restore the chosen second Israel and the Jewish nation was to return the global Canaan land centered around Jesus. But where did the chosen Israel nation, which bore this responsibility, go? And where did Judaism go? With the disappearance of the Israelite nation, the Jewish denomination, and the families of Israel, as well as the personal Israelites like Jacob and Moses, Jesus became a pitiful figure who died. He did not want to die. Today, established theologians mistakenly believe that He had to die. Pressured by the nation and denomination, betrayed by the twelve disciples, and ultimately betrayed by three disciples, He found no place to go but to die. The purpose of God sending Jesus was not for Him to live a pitiful life for over 30 years. Jesus was sent as the heavenly prince, the protagonist who could replace the ideology of creation. The suffering that the beloved Son of God, Jesus, faced on earth was not due to His wrongdoing. It was because the nation and denomination did not recognize Him, and society and family did not understand, leading Him down the path of suffering.

Thus, where is the Israel that Jesus sought, which committed the historical crime of killing Him? We must appeal to our hearts. And where is the Israel denomination that Jesus sought? We must pray from our hearts. You must understand that Jesus came to this earth 2000 years ago to seek the Israelite nation and denomination. Jesus died because the chosen first Israel opposed Him. Therefore, He established the second Israel, which replaces the lost first Israel, and is now working to re-establish it globally. This is precisely the time.

So what mission do Christian believers, who are scattered around the world today, have? Having lost the first chosen Israel by betraying Jesus and killing Him on the cross, the task of building the second Israel that replaces it remains for today's Christian believers.

345   Let us become the chosen Israel, the people of God. Today, where do the Christian believers scattered around the world stand? They must unite around figures like the twelve apostles of Jesus or the three disciples of Jesus as one denomination, but Christianity has lost this organization, which is a serious issue. The 600,000 people before Moses were able to pass through the wilderness because each had their position established within the ranks centered around the twelve tribal leaders and the seventy elders. However, the world Christians, who should bear the mission of becoming the second Israel, have no ranks. The twelve apostles and the three disciples, who appeared to replace the twelve ranks before Jesus, failed to take responsibility, leading to Jesus' death. Therefore, the global Christianity must recognize that the time is approaching to establish a representative denomination of the world centered around the twelve denominations.

What kind of life is Jesus living now? Since Jesus could not fulfill the heavenly will on this earth, just as Jacob and Moses lived as shepherds, Jesus is now in the spiritual realm living as a shepherd. He cannot rest in the spiritual realm and is praying for you, which is His shepherding life. What has He been doing? Throughout the 2000 years of history, Jesus has gathered those who believed in Him, that is, those who could become Israel, and has created the form of the lost second Israel in the spiritual realm, which is paradise. Having lost the first Israel that sought to kill Jesus, He gathered the saints who came before Him according to the principle of indemnity and restoration, and after Jesus' resurrection, the spiritual form of the first Israel restored today is the world of paradise.

What is the paradise world like? The spirits who have gone to paradise must establish the conditions to welcome Jesus on earth by receiving the blessings of the first Israel. Therefore, all spirits in heaven must return to earth and place the currently living Christians in a position to inherit the blessings of the second Israel, and they must work to indemnify the opposition of the first Israel to Jesus. You must understand this. However, today, Christians do not know this.

What time is it at the end? Just as the Gentile nations attacked the Jewish people who believed in the Old Testament, there will come a time when the Gentile nations will attack the Christians who believe in the New Testament. This is why the materialistic ideology centered around humanism is attacking Christianity. Even in the midst of this, a denomination that can hold onto the word must emerge, and that denomination must be a reformed denomination.

However, the Jewish people did not realize that when the time came to support the temple, they had to unite and fight. And when the time changed from supporting the temple to completing the substantial temple, there had to be a cosmic battle. Because they could not withstand this battle, it has now erupted globally. Similarly, at the end, you must prepare the substantial temple. And after establishing the substantial temple, what must be done? You must build the kingdom of heaven on earth.

Humans lost the word due to the fall. Therefore, the Old and New Testaments came out to guide humanity in a good direction, and now a new word will come to restore those who are united with that word in a substantial way. The feudal age was an era focused solely on God. Then, the Reformation occurred, which led to the understanding that God could be a being that could unite with humanity. Humanity has gone through this process, and now we are entering the era of restoring the substantial temple.

So what should you do in this time centered around the New Testament? When the ideology of a global covenant appears in the future, you must become the protagonists who can embrace the world and exist in place of Jesus. To become the protagonist of the kingdom of heaven on earth, after becoming the substantial temple, you must become the protagonist of your environment. To become such a being, you must go through the process of ideological revolution.

348   Let us become the chosen Israel, the people of God. So how will that process take shape? History will reap what it has sown, and even in today's global end times, those who belong to established beliefs and those who hold the words of established traditions are all in a position to betray heaven. Who are they? They are in a position like the archangel. Just as the archangel lured Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden, spiritual denominations similar to the archangel will inevitably appear in this end time, opposing God's will.

When we feel that God is restoring through these principles, how can we become the chosen Israelite nation at the end? You must make a resolution. You must prepare yourself. What kind of person should you become? You must become the heir of Jacob. You must become the representative of Jacob, who fought and believed by the Jabbok River for over 20 years, and you must be able to replace Moses, who walked while pleading with the Israelite nation in the wilderness, or Jesus, who prayed with concern for the Israelite nation representing the world in the Garden of Gethsemane.

The position of Christians in the last days. Now, O second Israel scattered around the world! Where is your place? The time has come for the Christian believers scattered around the world to appeal to heaven. Just as the Israelite nation, in distress, hated Pharaoh's palace in Egypt and searched for a leader to guide them to our promised land of Canaan, today’s Christians must also seek where their ranks and tribes should be.

For this reason, established churches will awaken. Only then can they be divided into twelve ranks. No matter how much you try to control it, because they are in a position to go through the global restoration destiny, even if it is a Christianity that moves the fate of nations, the time will come when it will lose its prestige in society, family, and individuals. Just as the Israelite nation did not organize ranks while in Egypt, they only organized ranks when it was time to depart for the wilderness. Similarly, global Christianity must now begin to organize ranks as the time for the second coming for the global return to Canaan approaches.

If Jesus had organized the ranks through the twelve disciples centered around Peter, John, and James, allowing any believer to belong to their tribe before He returned, today’s global Christianity would not be in confusion. The time is coming to reorganize this. However, there may come a time when a gathering that is rejected at the very bottom will be able to testify. The Unification Church might be such a church.

Now, in today’s Korean Christianity, there are people who claim to have spiritual experiences, such as Elder Na and Elder Park, and new denominations have emerged. Such factions are now breaking into the church. Since they must organize ranks, such movements are occurring. What remains as a problem here? It is the established ideology. This is an enemy before God. The established ideology, that is, the trivial thought that I, like Esau, am the firstborn and must receive God's blessing, must be discarded. If you are not careful, you will stand in the mindset of Esau and easily become the Jewish people who killed Jesus.

We have reached the end of history where we must overcome this, but how will we cross this threshold? At this time, who will be the enemy? Just as the archangel, who was closest to Adam in the Garden of Eden, became the enemy, the Jewish priests of that time, who corresponded to the archangel in the position of the second Adam who came to restore Adam, were the greatest enemies of Jesus. They took on the role of the archangel for the second time and attacked Jesus, so they must go to hell. 

Even today, at the end, the clergy scattered around the world will become archangels before the returning Lord, attacking heaven under the guise of heaven. However, even if they stand in such a position, they will not be influenced by the environment, and the historical fate will be overcome. Who will walk this path? New prophets who can declare a new end and fulfill their prophetic mission must emerge before this altar. However, they will have to be rejected by established denominations, thus moving on to a new stage.

At the same time, what era will come? The era of spiritual attacks will come. Just as the archangel tormented Jacob by the Jabbok River and attacked Moses and Jesus, there will come a time in the global end times when all people on earth will oppose and even attack heaven.

Faith that can escape the accusations of Satan. When Jesus was destined to die, He cried out, “My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?” (Matthew 27:46). Since Jesus appeared on behalf of the master of the universe's restoration, He had to indemnify Adam's betrayal of heaven on behalf of the universe. Even when Jesus was denied, He said He knew God, who said, “I do not know.” This condition of “knowing” could bring about spiritual resurrection. You must understand that there are historical turning points left in you as well. If you feel that the fate of the global end is seeping into your life today, you must understand that it is a sign of the time when Moses and the nation had to unite, and it is a sign of the time when Moses fought against Pharaoh.

Where did God's sorrow arise? It was not because the leaders were wrong that God was sorrowful, but because the people who followed them made God sorrowful. Today, what is your purpose in walking a path that others do not know, a path that others do not take? You must unite and become a rank that God can operate, becoming heirs who protect the footsteps of Moses, who struggled for the heavenly will, regardless of whether they eat or starve, and heirs of Jacob's footsteps, and you must fulfill your mission as heirs who follow the footsteps of Jesus. This is the end.
351 The conditions for the saints to enter the chosen Israel realm of the 351st day. Jesus, who represents heaven, understood this principle, which is why He said that those who want to live will die, and those who want to die will live. In other words, to subdue Satan, one must transcend even the realm of death centered on God. Even if heaven rejects humanity, one must be able to believe in heaven and step forward without being shaken; only then can Satan fall, and one can escape all accusations from Satan. Now, we must understand that heaven spiritually establishes the lost first Israel form, sets the world believers scattered across the globe as the second Israel, and manages the construction of the third Israel from the position where these two are united as one. Therefore, today you must become the ancestors of the third Israel like Abraham, become the ancestors of the third Israel instead of Jacob, become representatives of the third Israel like Moses, who was a national representative, and become representatives of the third Israel like Jesus, who was a world representative. Furthermore, you must recognize that you should become individuals, nations, and a world that can comfort God by stepping over Satan, who accused Father God in the past, while reflecting on the historical process of God's restoration providence. So, what is Satan? A traitor who opposes God. However, Satan also does not think God is bad. Therefore, God cannot help but deal with Satan. Satan also likes God. Because of this condition, it could not be avoided that 6,000 years have passed. Then, from Satan's perspective, who also likes God, he says, "Please let me be established to govern the universe through Adam, which is the purpose of governing all creation. Then I will absolutely obey before God." This means that Satan is working to make himself positive before God by opposing God's providential will to the end. Even the treacherous who pretend to be loyal do not dislike the king. However, they want to remove the loyal ones and have their own words listened to.

352 Since the chosen Israel, God's chosen people, stands in such a position, the whole world is within the realm of Satan. If this one thing is acknowledged, the world can return to God. But why can't it? Because it cannot violate the principles of heaven. God is a God of principles and cannot break order. Because of this, despite all efforts, God does not acknowledge Satan, who governs the world, and places people before Satan, who accuses them. This was God's sorrowful heart. If someone appears to stop Satan's accusations, they cannot say anything about God. Because the principles of heaven are restored, if there is a master who brings forth the principle that the archangel must be governed by Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden, all of Satan must fundamentally submit. This must also be established on earth, not in the spirit world, as it is not about going to God's throne like Jesus. The time to establish such a day is the age of the Second Coming. You should not stand in the position of opposing Satan now, but should follow the footsteps of God, who has labored for 6,000 years. You, at the end of the age, must experience God's heart, which has worked from the time of Adam, the first starting point of God's infinite world, to today, and must follow God's path. Despite being in such a destiny, you are not even dreaming, which is a serious problem. There must be a chosen Israel of heaven that can say, "O God! Be glorified through me and rest." This was the mission of Jacob, Moses, and Jesus. Only when you become a figure who can take over the fight that God fought against Satan can the decisive sovereignty of Israel be established before heaven. Thus, the purpose of the war that has accused God until now must be concluded. Because no objections can be raised, the war will end. It must be the time to start constructing the third Israel centered around such people.

353 In the time of Moses, the Israelite nation in Egypt had a battle left to attack their homeland, the welfare of Canaan, and in the time of Jesus, there was a battle left to build a global Canaan welfare centered on the Israelite nation. Today, for us who must construct the third Israel, there remains a fierce battle to unite and achieve the third Israel. So, what kind of people should you be today? When reorganizing the Israelite nation, you must voluntarily become a member of a trio, a squad leader, and a company, battalion, regiment, and division commander as the chosen people of Israel to be established before God. The question is, who will be the commanders of these heavenly soldiers? The time to do this will surely come. At the end of history, everything will be unified into one world. Many people are demanding ideological unity, and the earthly world is calling for a unifying ideology, so the time will come when the heavenly ideology can be communicated. In the historical process so far, what has happened? When two fight, a little good among them wins. That is the principle. When the earthly world enters a realm of one ideology, what will happen? A little good will win over the earthly. This is the era of spiritual attacks on the earth. Therefore, today, many neurotic diseases are occurring due to unknown reasons. Medicine will not work. This requires the heavenly duality medicine. The time has come for the spirit world to attack the earth for this ideology that can harmonize heaven and earth. Since earthly people are to represent God's will on earth, there will surely be a fight to become one. The world that becomes one after the two fight is the time of judgment when heaven becomes the center and unites. In this way, the one who will have the mission to represent the earth in the spirit world attacking the earth is the Lord of the Second Coming.

You, who stand at the starting point of the construction of the third Israel! What should you do? You must know the laws of the spirit world to escape. You must understand how the command system works. The army of that country must know the codes they are using to avoid being attacked by their own side during war. This is the time when the codes of the heavenly kingdom can be heard. Now is the era of coded communication. It is the era of providential codes, historical codes, temporal codes, human codes, and mission codes, and it is a time when communication can be made through these codes, operational plans can be executed, and the earthly unification ideology can be represented. Today, whether it is Elder Park, Elder Na, the Unification Church, or so-called heretical groups opposing the established church, it is fine. The modern era is discussing the cosmic age of science. It is the era of creating artificial suns. Having reached this era, you should not hold onto outdated religious concepts. A comprehensive unification ideology that can rise above this must emerge. Just as there are shortwave devices that can communicate codes today, if there is a possessor of a shortwave device that can communicate God's secrets, he will be victorious. Therefore, when the spirit world descends to attack the earth, the method of warfare will change. They will rise, but they will not know their limits. Such a battle will unfold on the earth, and at that time, conscientious people will be mobilized to join.

The path to becoming the ancestors of the third Israel. Now, you must understand that history has flowed until today, sacrificing conscientious good people to prepare for this one day at the end of the age. We, who are in the destiny of fall, must enter the ultimate ideal world and be able to forget everything and sacrifice. And we must become heavenly true sons and daughters who can confidently say, "God, please take charge of me," riding on the shoulders of Jesus. God is also hoping for such sons and daughters to appear. You must remember that the mission to introduce everything in the paradise world and the heavenly life is not with Jesus or God, but with you at the end of the age today. Only when a representative emerges who can take charge of all operational plans instead of Jesus and fight on behalf of God can we liberate God and Jesus. You must seek the victorious path of Israel in front of such a cosmic mission. To do this, you must find the ranks to which you belong and seek your leader. You must also understand what position you are in before heaven and become the unchanging representatives of Moses, Abraham, Jacob, and Jesus. Thus, when you command against Satan, you must become a being who can be worshiped by Satan with the praise that "You are the qualified son and daughter of God who can glorify God before Him on behalf of the creation ideology of the universe." Only then can you stand before God on the heavenly paradise as a representative of the global temple ideology.

Before that happens, you will face a great battle. Various denominations will attack you. You will also be spiritually tested. Just as God struck Moses, you will have such a path, and just as the nation betrayed Moses, there will be such a path before you. Just as Jesus was forsaken from heaven on the cross, there will be such things before you, and just as Jesus was betrayed by his nation, you will also have such paths. Knowing this, you must not be discouraged. The will of God is not an easy will; it is exceedingly difficult. Therefore, you must not fall in the path of battle while carrying the global tribulation and receiving extreme opposition. You must continue to struggle until the world and heaven and earth discover a common point. In this process, do not lament like the Israelite nation did when they left Egypt and complained about having no food or water in the wilderness. Do not blame others for not recognizing you. Think that it is best if I can just hold onto God, who recognizes me, and Jesus, who recognizes me. Believe that it is best to hold onto them and, even if everyone rejects you, if you hold onto them, you will inherit what they will accomplish. Only then can you qualify as the chosen people of the third Israel and participate in God's glory. Thus, you can become the appearance of God's glory, the historical glory, and the appearance of glory that can represent the ideology of the entire universe. In other words, we must appear before heaven as glorious sons and daughters representing the world so that God can finally rest.

It will not be the blessing that the angel gave to Jacob, but the blessing that God Himself wanted to bless Jesus by raising His hand. That is, to you, who have reached the end of the age, God will bless you to be my sons and daughters as the protagonists of the eternal third Israel, who have replaced Jesus, and will bless you to become the substantial joy, glory, and beauty that heaven can rejoice in forever. In this way, through the love of Jesus, you must enter into the realm of God's love and fulfill God's love to become the ancestors of the third Israel. 

<Prayer> In the spirit world, ranks are organized in the name of the second Israel, but today, the Christianity scattered across the world has not formed the ranks of the second Israel. Father! Awaken the sleeping nations and awaken the sleeping Christians of the world, and create ranks that can replace the blessings of the second Israel on earth, so that the spirit world can unite and grant us the right to construct the third Israel globally today. Thus, through the organized tribes, nations, and eventually the world, may we inherit the heavenly mission that must pass through, and may we inherit the path that Moses fought, and may we inherit the path that Jesus fought, overcoming the accusations and slanders of Satan, and may we be allowed to serve the Father and receive the glory of the Father. Father, we earnestly desire and wish for this. We sincerely hope that, through the words delivered today, you will raise us as joyful sons and daughters who can overcome the suffering of the chosen people of Israel, and allow them to achieve the global Canaan restoration path. Now, in the path of battle against Satan, may we unite and win, and may we not become a group that rebels against the central will of Jesus, and may we not become a group that causes suffering to the center. Although the nation was one that criticized Moses, we know that heaven needed it for the construction of Israel. Now, we earnestly ask that we may become sons and daughters who can achieve the third Israel without causing heaven any concern, and we pray all these words in the name of the Lord. Amen.
